ACT 7:41 Ye wode hyarina aazizi eequntsana medhdhida. Yentsi eequntsis zharsho zharshi fa kushite oochchide oochita un qoftti fana hyanide gisho ufayttida.
ACT 7:42 Yezin Xoozii unttis bantte mahida. Un salo xoolintto goynode gaar unttana olii ashshida. Nabunts maxaafite, « ‹Isra7eele asuntso, oyttam bere ubba akko baayze ganas sa7a shukkide hyarsin zharshide zharshito taas shiishidaane?
ACT 7:43 Yin, yinttis goynodes kesside Moloke dunkkaane Refaane ga7inttize yin eeqize xoolintto misile tukkida. Ta yinttana Baabilooneppa gode dakkoda› ga7intti xaafinttida.
ACT 7:44 «Nu aduntsis akko baayze ganasa markka dunkkaane yene. Ezan Xoozii Muse kiittidannigaaran eza beezidanni gaaran medhdhida.
ACT 7:45 Mahi nu aduntsi yinna dunkkaantto fa aduntsappa ekkii Xoozii tiino bay7ide Ayhude maaqqoosse asunts gadito aykkide wode Iyyaasura yeyga ekkii gelida. Ye dunkkaaniza Dawute wode yellodes yinna besite yezida.
ACT 7:46 Dawute Xoozappa nashshinttida. Mahi Yayqooba Xoozzes yessade keetstsi keexades Xooz woossida.
ACT 7:47 Yezin eesi keetstsi keexxide Solomona.
ACT 7:48 «Maaqqikon, Ubbappa kattara yeze Xoozze asi keexxide keetstsa yezoos. Nabize gaydanni gaar,
ACT 7:49 « ‹Salo taas araata, sa7an ta tohita yedhdhize bessi. Yeezin, taas yin akko gaarize keetstsi keexxode? Woy ta shemppize besita aba?
ACT 7:50 Hyanno ubba ta kushite medhdhika?› yagayda Laatstsi.
ACT 7:51 «Yin wayde si7oosse aso? Yin wozintta Xoozze qaala ekkodes akkosi ixxido? Yin hyayta akkosi tullido? Yin, yin aduntsi gaar ubba wode Geeshi Ayyaana ixxane.
ACT 7:52 Nabunts giddappa yin aduntsi bay7ikaayze oode? Xillizay yo7odanno tiinidhii ohiduntsana wodhida. Hyatte yin eza aatsii inggi wodhida.
ACT 7:53 Yin Kiitanchcho kusheppa Xoozze higgito ekkida, yezin kiitinttikaaya» yagayda.
ACT 7:54 Un yinno si7ide wode fa wozintte Isxifaanosalla gaama zhilidhdhi, fa doontto dha7i manddida.
ACT 7:55 Yezin Isxifaanosa Geeshi Ayyaanara kumii, Salo ude bi7i, Xoozze bonchchiton Yesuusa Xoozze mizaqi zalara eqqidanno bi7ida.
ACT 7:56 «Yikke, taanii salo bugunttin, As Na7ay, Xoozze mizaqi zalara eqqidaya bi7ida» yagayda.
ACT 7:57 Fa qaaltto dhoqi yiizii wuysittera, fa hyayito aykkii fettilla eego woxxida
ACT 7:58 Eza katamappa gaxa kessii, shuchchara dhogida. Markkuntsi fa ma7ito fettii Saawula gaaze na7atitsi atstse kale gaddida.
ACT 7:59 Isxifaanosa, «Ta Laatstso Yesuusa, ta shemppito ekko» yaga7i xeegodera un eza shuchchara dhogane.
ACT 7:60 Bunqqunttii, fa qaaltto dhoqi yiizii, «Ta Laatstsayo, hyanna nagartto unttis atto ga7o» yagayda. Yinno yaga7i maaqqii hyayqqida.
ACT 8:1 Saawula Isxifaanosa wodhe qofite gelida. Ye wode Yerusalaame yeze woosa keetstsite damma bay7e denddida. Hawaaruntsap attin ammanze ubbuntsi Yihuda sa7an Samaara sa7a lalinttida.
ACT 8:2 Fettii fettii Xooz asuntsi Isxifaanosa moogida; mahi ees damma yeekkida.
ACT 8:3 Yezin Saawula woosa keetsito lalodes koyane. Ubbunts kara wutii gelii, ammanze dhiiratsuntsanan maachuntsana gochchii kessii achi keetstsa geltsane.
ACT 8:4 Lalinttide ammanzuntsi qitide bessa ubba qaala ohine.
ACT 8:5 Filphoosa Samaara katama gelii Kiristtoosa baz asuntsis ohida.
ACT 8:6 Gaama asuntsi Filphoosa gaydanno si7ide woden E oochchide kille bazito bi7ide woden eza akaakii si7ida.
ACT 8:7 Tuna ayyaana uukki gaama asuntsappa kezida; mahi gaama tohe gundduntsin wobbuntsin bilinttida.
ACT 8:8 Yinna katamite yeze asuntsi damma ufayttida.
ACT 8:9 Yezin Simoona gaaze fettii atstse yinna katamite yene. E, Taanii damma ga7i Samaara asuntsana maridhdhitera gaama qofizittera gam77ida.
ACT 8:10 Eeratsappa damma yellodes yeze asuntsana ubba, «Damma Xoozze wolqqita hyanno» ga7i eza si7ine.
ACT 8:11 Gaama wodeppa aykkii maridhittera Samaara asuntsana gaama qofize gisho asuntsi eza si7ine.
ACT 8:12 Yezin Filphoosa Xoozze ka7itumon Yesuus Kiristtoosa suntsitibaz dhiiratsuntsisin maachuntsis ohin, un E baz ammanii xammaqinttida.
ACT 8:13 Mahi Simoonan fa ommite ammanii xammaqinttida. Filphoosar wolla hyanggide bessa ubba oochinttize damma kille baz bi7i gaama qoppida.
ACT 8:14 Yerusalaame yeze hawaaruntsi Samaara asuntsi Xoozze qaala ekkidanno si7ide wode Phexiroosan Wahannisan unttago dakkida.
ACT 8:15 Phexiroosan Wahannisan hyanggi, ammanzuntsi Geeshi Ayyaana ekkode gaar unttis Xooz woossida.
ACT 8:16 Akkos gayko, Samaara asuntsi Laatstse Yesuusa suntsite xalaala xammaqinttidap attin unttappa fetellan Geeshi Ayyaana hyaga wodhdhikaaya.
ACT 8:17 Ye wode Phexiroosan Wahannisan fa kushito unttalla gaddin, un Geeshi Ayyaana ekkida.
ACT 8:18 Hawaaruntsi fa kushito unttalla gaddin, unttis Geeshi Ayyaana ingginttidanno Simoona bi7ide wode Phexiroosasin Wahannisas miishe ki7i,
ACT 8:19 «Taanin ta kushito gaddize ubbuntsi Geeshi Ayyaana ekkode fana hyanna adetits wolqqito taasin inggoya» yagayda.
ACT 8:20 Yezin Phexiroosa eego, «Ne Xoozze imotitsi miishera ekkodes qoppide gisho ne miishita neera dhabo.
ACT 8:21 Ne wozintta Xoozze tiino likke maaqqikaayze gisho nees hyanne gisho woy ixa baaya.
ACT 8:22 Yikke, hyanna ne wozina iitatitsiti gisho nagarttippa maaqqo. Ne wozintte yeze iita qoftto Xoozii atto gawude gaar Laatstsa woosso.
ACT 8:23 Akkos gayko, neenii iita ixxeran nagara achchara yezanno ta be7ine» gayda.
ACT 8:24 Simoona mahi, «Yin ga7idannippa fettin tana yellaame gaar taas Laatstsa woossote» yagayda.
ACT 8:25 Phexiroosan Wahannisan markkidhidannippan Laatstse qaala ohidannippa suuba Yerusalaame maaqqida. Samaara yeze gaama guta Wonggele ohida.
ACT 8:26 Laatstse kiitanchcho Filphoosago, «Denddii Yerusalaameppa Gaaza kanggize akko baayze ganasa ogizera hyanggo. Yinna ogita yeekka zalara yene» gayda.
ACT 8:27 Filphoosa denddii qitida. Hinddeko gaaze Tophphe kaattis I miishito ubba naagize Tophphe asi yene. Ezin goynodes Yerusalaame yi7ida.
ACT 8:28 Fara gaarella bettii, Yerusalaameppa fa sa7a maaqqitera nabe Isayaasa maxaafe nabbabane.
ACT 8:29 Geeshi Ayyaana Filphoosago, «Ye gaarizego hyanggi E kale shiiqo» yagayda.
ACT 8:30 Yeezin Filphoosa woxxii hyanggi yellize wode moorinnize nabe Isayaasa maxaafeppa nabbabodera si7i, «Ne nabbabizanna nees gelane?» yagayda.
ACT 8:31 Moorinnize «Taas ohi geltsize as baayzin wayzi gelode?» yagayda. Fara gaarzella kezii bettode fana Filphoosa woossida.
ACT 8:32 Moorinnize nabbabize maxaafe kifilize, «E duro fana shukinttodes izhinttida; Duro na7a fa isintsito meedizunts tiino si77i gaazanni fana, ezin fa doontto bugikaaya.
ACT 8:33 E toochinttida; ees xillo firdda dhabida. E de7ita hyanna sa7itippa hyal7ide gisho E yeletuntsappa oonii ohode?» gayda.
ACT 8:34 Moorinnize mahi Filphoosago, «Nabize obaz ohe? Fa baz ohinen woy melle asi baz ohine? Taas ohoya» gayda.
ACT 8:35 Filphoosa mahi, Xoozze qaala yinna besstippa aykkii, Yesuusa baz ohize Wonggele ees ohida.
ACT 8:36 Un hyanggiter hyaatsi yeze bessa yellida. Moorinnize, «Hyaatsi hyanno bo7o; ta xammaqinttaame fana akko kayze?» gayda.
ACT 8:37 Filphoosa eego, «Neenii ne kumutsi wozinappa ammaniko dandda7ane» gayda. E mahi, «Yesuus Kiristtoosa Xoozze Na7a maaqqidanno ta ammanane» gayda.
ACT 8:38 Gaarize eqqode fana moorinnize kiittin, lam77untsi wodhdhii hyaatstsa gelida; Filphoosan eza xammaqida.
ACT 8:39 Un hyaatsitippa gaxa kezide wode Laatstse Ayyaana Filphoosa qoppikaayzin ekkida. Lam7intsa moorinnize Filphoosa bi7ikaaya, yezin fa ogito ufayttiter qitida.
ACT 8:40 Filphoosa Azaaxone benttida. Mahi Qisaariya ye7ode wontsis katamar wutii Wonggele markkidhida.
ACT 9:1 Ye wode Saawula Laatstsi tamaaruntsana wodhodes manddii kahinunts hyalaqizego qitida.
ACT 9:2 Laatstse ogito kaallize dhiiratsuntsanan maachuntsana denggiko, accitera Yerusalaame ko7odes, Demasqqo yeze Ayhude woosa Keetstsis dabddaabbe xaafinttode gaar eza woossida.
ACT 9:3 E hyanggi, Demasqqo katama yellodes ukkodera, qoppikaayzin saloppa damma foo7o E kantte foo7ida.
ACT 9:4 E sa7ite gol7in, «Saawula, Saawula, akkos tana bay7e?» gaaze qaala si7ida.
ACT 9:5 Saawula, «Laatstso, ne oode?» yaga7i oocida. «Taanii, ne bay7ize Yesuusa» yagayda.
ACT 9:6 Laatstsi eego, «Denddii katama gelo; ne oochchodes koshshize baz ize nees ohoda» yagayda.
ACT 9:7 Saawulara ogito hyanggize asuntsi akkon ohikaayzara eqqii attida. Ootsito si7ine, yezin oona yezakon bi7ikaaya.
ACT 9:8 Saawula gol7ide bessitippa denddii be7ize wode E aafita dengganxida. Yinnii gisho, un E kushito aykkii kaalitsi Damasqqo geltsida.
ACT 9:9 Hyaydzdzii qamma yellodes E be7ades dandda7ikaaya; akkon mu7ikaaya; uzhikaaya.
ACT 9:10 Damasqqo gidda fettii Hananiya gaaze Yesuusa tamaarize yene. Laatstsi qonccitsara, «Hananiya» yaga7i xeegida. Hananiya mahi, «Ta Laatstso, yoo» yagayda.
ACT 9:11 Laatstsii eego, «Denddii moolo ga7inttize ogito hyanggi, Yihuda keetstsa Saawula gaaze Terseseppa ye7eze atstsa koyo; Saawula hyatte woosalla yene.
ACT 9:12 Mahi Hananiya gaaze atstse gelii, Saawula lam7intsa be7ade gaar fa kushito eella gaddodera qonccitsara bi7ida» yagayda.
ACT 9:13 Hananiya mahi, «Laatstso, Yerusalaame ne geeshi asuntsalla ye atstse akko gaar iita baz oochchezako ta gaama asappa si7ida.
ACT 9:14 Mahi Damasqqo gidda ne suntsito xeegizuntsana ubba accodes, kahinunts hyalaquntsi ees adetits wolqqa inggidda» yagayda.
ACT 9:15 Yezin Laatstsi eego, «Saawula Ayhude maaqqoosse asunts tiino, kaatuntsi tiinon Isra7eele asunts tiinon, ta suntsito tookkodesin taas oochchodes doorinttide miishe maaqqide gisho ne eego qito.
ACT 9:16 Akkos gayko, ta suntsiti gisho E wantsi madha ekkodes koshshizako ta eza beessada» yagayda.
ACT 9:17 Hananiya hyanggi, keetstsa gelii, fa kushito Saawulalla gaddii, «Ta ishe Saawula, ne yi7ize ogite nees benttide E Laatstse Yesuusa, ne be7ade gaaran Geeshi Ayyaanara kumode gaar tana kiittida» gayda.
ACT 9:18 Ellisii, Saawula afttippa fettii quro fana yeze baz wodhdhin, Saawula lam7intsa bi7ida. Mahi denddii xammaqinttida.
ACT 9:19 Katstsa mu7i minggida. Damasqqo gidda yeze tamaarutsara eeratsi qamma gam77ida.
ACT 9:20 Ellisii Saawula, «Yesuusa Xoozze Na7a» yaga7i Damasqqo gidda yeze Ayhude woosa keetstsa qaala tamaarssida.
ACT 9:21 Yinno si7ize ubbuntsi qoppii, «Hyay Yerusalaame Yesuusa suntsito xeegizuntsana bay7izaya baane? Mahi hyayga yi7idanna unttana accii, kahinunts hyalaquntsi tiino kanggodes baane?» yagayda.
ACT 9:22 Yezin Saawula qaala ohera miinggiter hyanggida. Yesuusa, E Kiristtoosa maaqqidanno qonccizi ohide gisho Damasqqo gidda yeze Ayhuduntsi ees mahodebaz dhabida.
ACT 9:23 Gaama qammappa maaqqii Ayhuduntsi shiiqii, Saawula wodhodes zorinttida.
ACT 9:24 Yezin Ayhuduntsi fana wodhodes qoppidanno Saawula erida. Un eza wodhodes qamman awaran katama furtsite naagane.
ACT 9:25 Mahi E tamaaruntsi eza qamma kanggi, gimbbe gase wulunqqera kessii daachchora ketstsida.
ACT 9:26 Saawula Yerusalaame yellide wode ammanzuntsara yellinttodes qoppida. Yezin E Kiristtoosa ammanidanna unttis turo aazanxi ixxin ees zhashtida.
ACT 9:27 Yezin Barnnabaasa Saawula hawaaruntsago kanggida. Oge Laatstsi wayzi qonccezakon ohizezako, mahi Saawula Damasqqo gidda Yesuusa suntsite zhashtikaayzara wayzi qaala ohezako unttis geeshi ohida.
ACT 9:28 Saawula Yerusalaame wutii Laatstse suntsite zhashtikaayzara qaala ohitera, hawaaruntsara wolla yezida.
ACT 9:29 Mahi Saawula Girike doona ohize Ayhuduntsara ohintti lallida. Yezin un eza wodhodes koyda.
ACT 9:30 Ammanze asuntsi yinno si7i, Saawula Qisaariya kanggi Terseese dakkida.
ACT 9:31 Yihuda, Galilan Samaaran ubba gidda yeze woosa keetsita sarora yezida. Mahi minggida; Laatstsis zhashtiter Geeshi Ayyaana miintsitsodera gaanggitter hyanggida.
ACT 9:32 Phexiroosa sa7a ubba wutii Liida yeze ammanze asuntsago yellida.
ACT 9:33 Ize osfun bere kumutsi wobbii yiitsa woy7i yeze Eeniya gaaze atstsa denggida.
ACT 9:34 Phexiroosa, «Eeniya, Yesuus Kiristtoosa nena fatstsoda; denddii ne yitsito dentso» yagayda. Ezin ellisii denddii eqqida.
ACT 9:35 Liidan Saaronan yeze asuntsi ubba Eeniya bi7i, Laatstsago maaqqida.
ACT 9:36 Iyoophe katama fettii Xaabito gaaze ammanzanna yene. (Xaabito ga7inttizanna gen77e ga7intte) Iza fa yezide wodite ubba lo77o baz oochiteran dahuntsana maaddite yezida.
ACT 9:37 Ye wode iza hyargginttii hyayqqin, asuntsi I ahito meeccii, fooqella kessii woytstsida.
ACT 9:38 Liida Iyoophes kale. Ammanzuntsi Phexiroosa Liida yezanno si7i, «Woy7a nuugo ellisii yo7o» yagaaze kiita lam77i asara eego kiittida.
ACT 9:39 Yinnii gisho, Phexiroosa denddii, unttara qitida. Yeyga yellin, fooqella yeze kifilite eza geltsida. Azini baayze maachuntsi Phexiroosa kantte eqqii yeekkitera Dorqqa unttara faxa yezitera oochchide qamistton afultto ubba Phexiroosa beezida.
ACT 9:40 Phexiroosa unttana ubba bale kessii, bunqqunttii Xooz woossida. Mahi ahitigo maaqqii, «Xaabite, denddo» yagayda. Xaabita fa aafto bugii Phexiroosa bi7i, denddii bettida.
ACT 9:41 Phexiroosa izo fa kushite katizii dentsii essida. Yinnippa maaqqii, ammanzuntsanan azinii baayzuntsana xeegii, un tiino shiishida.
ACT 9:42 Hyanna ohita Iyoophe katama ubba yellida. Gaama asuntsi Laatstsa ammanida.
ACT 9:43 Phexiroosa Iyoophe Simoona gaaze qole hyaashize kara gaama wode gam77ida.
ACT 10:1 Qisaariya, «Xaaliya ola asuntsana» ga7inttize olinttizunts gidda fettii Qornneliyoosa ga7inttize mato hyalaqa yene.
ACT 10:2 Qornneliyoosa fa kara asuntsara Xooz goynizen zhashtize asi, dahuntsanan maaddane, mahi ubba wode Xooz woossane.
ACT 10:3 Fettii wode uddufun saate kumizin Xooz kiitanchcho eego yi7i, «Qornneliyoosa» ga7i xeegodera E qonccitsara geeshi bi7ida.
ACT 10:4 Qornneliyoosa zhashtii Kiitanchchiza dakkii loytsii bi7i, «Laatstso, yinna akko?» yagayda. Kiitanchchize mahi, «Ne woositan dahuntsana ne maaddidanna Xoozze tiino qofinttes yellida.
ACT 10:5 Hyatte asuntsana Iyoophe dakkii, Phexiroosa gaaze Simoona ki7izo.
ACT 10:6 Phexiroosa abba gaxa qole hyaashize Simoona kara zaqqottetsi bettida» gayda.
ACT 10:7 Qornneliyoosa faas ohide kiitanchchize qitin, fa aruntsappa lam77untsana Xooz goynize fa kale wottaddaruntsappa feta xeegii,
ACT 10:8 unttis ohi Iyoophe kiittida.
ACT 10:9 Wonttisti wode un hyanggi, Iyoophe katama ukkodera izipun saate gaar yezin Xooz woossodes Phexiroosa fooqella kezida.
ACT 10:10 E naydhdhii katstsa maades koyda, yezin katstsa kaxxodera E ayyaanara maaqqii qonccitsi bi7ida.
ACT 10:11 Salo bugunttin, damma afula aazize baz oyddii zalara aykkinttii wodhdhodera E bi7ida.
ACT 10:12 Iza besite oyddii tohera yeze gurdde xootsi, sazara gochinttize medhetitsin salo landda ubba yene.
ACT 10:13 Ye wode «Phexiroosa, denddii eqqii shukkii mo7o» gaaze qaala eego yi7ida.
ACT 10:14 Yezin Phexiroosa, «Laatstso, ade! Ta tuna baz mulon mu7i eroos» gayda.
ACT 10:15 Mahi, «Xoozii geeshidanno ne tuna ga7ippe» gaaze qaala lam7intsa eego yi7ida.
ACT 10:16 Yinnan, hyaydzdzii tohe yi7idannippa maaqqii ye damma afula aazize ellisii ude salo ekinttida.
ACT 10:17 Phexiroosa fa be7eze qonccitsiti bilitsita, «Akko maaqqad yessa?» ga7i fa wozintte qoppodera, Qornneliyoosa kiitteze asuntsi Simoona kara oocii denggi bale eqqida.
ACT 10:18 Fa qaaltto un dhoqi yiizii, «Phexiroosa gaaze Simoona zaqqotits yeze hyanne yene?» yaga7i oocida.
ACT 10:19 Phexiroosa qonccitsara bi7idanno tawodera, Geeshi Ayyaana eego, «Hyaychche, hyaydzdzii asuntsi nena koyane.
ACT 10:20 Denddii wodhdho, ta unttana kiitteze gisho so7ikaayzara unttara qito» yagayda.
ACT 10:21 Phexiroosa asuntsago wodhdhii, «Yin koyze tana; akkos yi7idote?» yagayda.
ACT 10:22 Un mahi, «Nuna mato hyalaqize Qornneliyoosa kiittida. E xillo, Xooz goynize asin Ayhude asunts gidda ubba gaama bonchchinttide asi. Qornneliyoosa, nena fa kara ki7izii qaala neeppa si7ode fana geeshi kiitanchcho ees ohida» yagayda.
ACT 10:23 Phexiroosa asuntsana kara geltsii mokkida. Wonttisti wode, denddii unttara qitida. Yoophe katama yeze ammanzuntsappa fettii fettii asunts eera wolla qitida.
ACT 10:24 Wonttistti wode, Qisaariya yellida. Qornneliyoosa fa iginuntsanan fa kale lagguntsana fettilla xeegii shiishii, Phexiroosa naagane.
ACT 10:25 Phexiroosa kara gelodes yi7adera, Qornneliyoosa eera yellintti E tiino gol7i ees goynodes koyda.
ACT 10:26 Yezin Phexiroosa, «Denddo, taanin ta ommite ne gaar asi» yaga7i eza dentstsida.
ACT 10:27 Phexiroosa Qornneliyoosara ohitera kara gelize wode gaama asuntsi shiiqidanno denggida.
ACT 10:28 E asuntsago, «Ayhude asi melle worzhara wolla maaqqades woy yellinttodes woga baayzanno yin erane. Yezin taanii ooden tuna woy geeshi ga7aame gaar Xoozii tana beezida.
ACT 10:29 Yinnii gisho, yin taago kiittin ixxikaayzara yi7ida. Hyatte tana akkos xeegizezako taas ohote» yagayda.
ACT 10:30 Qornneliyoosa, «Taanii hyayno oyddii qammappa tiino hyannii wode uddufun saate woosa woossodera, foo7ize ma7o ma77ide asi ta tiino eqqida.
ACT 10:31 E taago, ‹Qornneliyoosa, Xoozii ne woosito si7ida, neenii dahuntsana maaddidanno qoppida.
ACT 10:32 Yikke, asi Yoophe kiittii, Simoon Phexiroosa gaazaya xeegizo. E, Simoona gaaze qole hyaashize atstse kara abba gaxa bettida› yagayda.
ACT 10:33 Yinnii gisho, ta neego ellisii kiittida; ne yi7idanna lo77o. Yikke, Xoozii nena Kiittidebaz ubba si7odes hyatte nu ubbuntsi hyanne Laatstse tiino yene» yagayda.
ACT 10:34 Kaallii, Phexiroosa, «Xoozii asis sino bi7i asi asappa shagoos.
ACT 10:35 Yezin asi ubba oona maaqqikon faas zhashtizayan xillo oocha oochchizella Xoozii ufayttizanno ta turo qoppida.
ACT 10:36 Xoozii, ubbuntsi Laatstsii maaqqide Yesuus Kiristtoosa baggara sarotitsi ohitera hyanna wonggeltto Isra7eele asuntsis kiittezanno yin erane.
ACT 10:37 Wahannisa xinqqate baz sabbakide wodeppa aykkii Galilan Yihuda sa7a ubba yellodes hyanidanno yin erane.
ACT 10:38 Xoozii Naazirete Yesuusa Geeshi Ayyaanara tizhii wolqqa inggida. Xoozii eera yeze gisho lo77o baz E oochchitera Xalahe kushe aqiduntsana ubba fatstsitera wutida.
ACT 10:39 «Ayhude sa7an Yerusalaame E oochchide ubbabazitis nu markka. Un masqalalla suxxii eza wodhida.
ACT 10:40 Yezin Xoozii hyaydzdzintsa wode hyayqoppa eza dentsii asuntsis qonccode gaar yiizida.
ACT 10:41 Yinna qonccitsita Xoozii tiino dooride markkuntsis fattin as ubbas maaqqoos. E hyayqoppa denddidannippa maaqqii eera mu7i uzhida.
ACT 10:42 Nu Wonggele asuntsis ohode gaaran faxa yezuntsallan hyayqqiduntsalla firddodes Xoozii shuumide Yesuusa maaqqizanno markkidhade gaar nuna kiittida.
ACT 10:43 Xoozii eza ammanize ubba nagartta, E suntsite atto ga7inttizanno nabuntsi markkidhane» yagayda.
ACT 10:44 Phexiroosa hyaga yinna ohito hyaasikaayzin qaala si7ize ubbuntsalla Geeshi Ayyaana wodhdhida.
ACT 10:45 Phexiroosara Yoopheppa yi7ide ammanize garrazinttide Ayhude ubbuntsallan, Ayhude maaqqoosuntsallan Geeshi Ayyaana wodhdhidanno bi7i gaama qoppida.
ACT 10:46 Akkos gayko, un melle melle doonara ohiteran Xoozze dammatitsito sabbodera si7ida. Ye wode Phexiroosa mahi,
ACT 10:47 «Hyantses mahi nu gaar Geeshi Ayyaana ekkiduntsi xammaqinttaame gaar hyaatsi kayode oode?» yagayda.
ACT 10:48 Un Yesuus Kiristtoosa suntsite xammaqinttode gaar unttana kiittida. Yinnippa maaqqii, un faara eerats wode bettode gaar Phexiroosa woossida.
ACT 11:1 Hawaaruntsin Yihuda yeze ammanzuntsi, Ayhude maaqqoosuntsin Xoozze qaala ekkidanno si7ida.
ACT 11:2 Phexiroosa Yerusalaame qitide wode garrazinttide ammanzuntsi,
ACT 11:3 eego, «Ne garrazinttikaayzuntsago gelii unttara katstsa akkos mu7ido?» ga7i lallida.
ACT 11:4 Yezin Phexiroosa hyanidanno tiinoppa aykkii tarar tarar ohida:
ACT 11:5 «Taanii Yoophe katama Xooz woossittera qonccitsi bi7ida. Damma afula aazize baz oyddii zalara aykkinttii saloppa wodhdhitera taago yi7ida.
ACT 11:6 Taanii dakkii loytsii E gidito be7ize wode oyddii tohera yeze gurdde xootsuntsi, sazara gochinttize medhon salo landduntsana bi7ida.
ACT 11:7 ‹Phexiroosa, denddii, shukkii mo7o› gaaze qaala si7ida.
ACT 11:8 «Yezin taanii, ‹Laatstso, ade, tuna baz woy geezhikaayzebaz mulon doonago shiishii eroos› yagayda.
ACT 11:9 « ‹Xoozii geeshidanno neenii tuna ga7ippe› yagaaze qaala lam7intsa saloppa yi7ida.
ACT 11:10 «Yinna hyaydzdzii tohe hyanidannippa suuba, maaqqii ubba bazita salo ude ekinttida.
ACT 11:11 Yinna saate hyaydzdzii asuntsi Qisaariyappa taago kiitinttii ta yeze keetstsite yellida.
ACT 11:12 So7ikaayzara unttara qitode gaar Ayyaana taas ohida. Mahi hyanna izippun ishuntsi Yoopheppa taara Qisaariya hyanggiduntsara Qornneliyoosa kara gelida.
ACT 11:13 Kiitanchcho E kara eqqii, ‹Yoophe kiittii Phexiroosa ga7inttize Simoona xeegizo.
ACT 11:14 Nenan ne kara as ubba ashshize qaala E nees ohoda› gaydanno Qornneliyoosa nuus ohida.
ACT 11:15 «Taanii ohe aykkize wode Geeshi Ayyaana tiino nuulla wodhdhidannigaara unttallan wodhdhida.
ACT 11:16 Ye wode ‹Wahannisa hyaatsara xammaqida, yezin yin Geeshi Ayyaanara xammaqinttoda› yagayde Laatstse qaaltta taas tiirinttida.
ACT 11:17 Xoozii nuus Laatstse Yesuus Kiristtoosa ammanzuntsis inggide imotitsito mahi izo Ayhude maaqqoosuntsisin inggiko, yeezin Xooz kayodes ta oode?» yagayda.
ACT 11:18 Un yinno si7ide wode fa lallizanno ashshii, «Yinno maaqqiko, Xoozii Ayhude maaqqoosuntsin nagarappa maaqqii de7o yessade gaar ixa inggida» yaga7i Xooz galatida.
ACT 11:19 Isxifaanosa hyayqos yeltside bay7e gisho lalinttide ammanzuntsi qaala Ayhudunts xalaalas ohitera Siroofinqe, Qoophiroosan Anxookiyan yellodes wutida.
ACT 11:20 Yezin Qoophiroosappan Qereenappan yi7ide fettii fettii ammanize asuntsi Anxookiya hyanggi, Laatstsi Yesuusa Wonggele Girike asuntsis ohida.
ACT 11:21 Laatstse wolqqa unttara yene; mahi gaama asuntsi ammanii Laatstsago maaqqida.
ACT 11:22 Yinna ohito Yerusalaame yeze woosa keetsita si7ide gisho Barnnabaasa Anxookiya kiittida.
ACT 11:23 Barnnabaasa Anxookiya qitide wode Xoozze aadho keehatitsi oocha bi7i ufayttida. Un ubbuntsi fa kumutsi wozintte Laatstse gidda miinggi yessade gaar unttana zorida;
ACT 11:24 yinnii gisho Barnnabaasa Geeshi Ayyaanaran ammanora kumide lo77o asi. Gaama asuntsi Laatstsa ammanida.
ACT 11:25 Yinnippa maaqqii, Barnnabaasa Saawula koyodes Terseese qitida.
ACT 11:26 Ize Saawula denggide wode Anxookiya ekkii yi7ida. Barnnabaasan Saawula woosa keetstsi asuntsara fettii bere mulo bettii gaama asuntsana tamaarssida. Tamaaruntsi Anxookiya woosa keetstsa «Kiristtaane» ga7intti tiinii xeeginttida.
ACT 11:27 Ye wode fettii fettii nabuntsi Yerusalaameppa Anxookiya wodhdhida.
ACT 11:28 Un giddappa Agaboosa ga7inttize denddii sa7a ubba damma naye kessadanno Ayyaana wolqqara tinbbite ohida. Yinna hyanidanna Roome Kaat Qalawudiyoosa wode.
ACT 11:29 Ammanzuntsi fete fete fa wolqqiti gaar miishe kessii Yihuda yeze ammanzutsis maade dakkodes qofa accida.
ACT 11:30 Un hyannigaara yeyzi, miishito Barnnabaasaran Saawularan woosa keetstsa cimuntsis dakkida.
ACT 12:1 Ye wode Kaat Heroodisa woosa keetstsi asuntsappa bagguntsana bay7e aykkida.
ACT 12:2 Wahannisa ishe Yayqooba mashshara wodhida.
ACT 12:3 Yinna Ayhuduntsana ufayssidanno bi7i, gujjii Phexiroosan aytsida. Yinna hyanidanna boora Ba7ale bonchchize qammite.
ACT 12:4 Phexiroosa aykkii accida. Faasiga bonchchize woditippa maaqqii worzhunts tiino aatsodes qoppii, oyddii oyddii wottaddaruntsi eza naagode gaar taphpho izippun wottaddaruntsis aatsii inggida.
ACT 12:5 Yinnii gisho, Phexiroosa achi keetstsa naaginttane. Yezin woosa keetstsa asuntsi ees mintsii Xooz woossane.
ACT 12:6 Heroodisa Phexiroosa asunts tiino shiishodannippa tiino qamma Phexiroosa lam77i zalara lam77i wottaddaruntsaran lam77i santsalaatara acinttii un gidda genttida. Naagizuntsi achi keetstsa furtsite eqqii naagane.
ACT 12:7 Tiirikaayzin Laatstse kiitanchcho benttida. Achi keetstsa foo7o foo7ida. Kiitanchchize Phexiroosa millito bochchii barkkizii, «Elle denddo» yagayda. Iira santsalaatan E kushtippa wodhdhida.
ACT 12:8 Kiitanchchize eego, «Ne ma7ito ma77o, ne caammiton aatso» yagayda. Phexiroosa hyannigaara oochchida; kiitanchchize, «Ne laxinza ma77i tana kaallo» yagayda.
ACT 12:9 Phexiroosa achi keetstsappa kezii kiitanchchiza kaallida. Ees qonccitsi be7izegaara yi7idap attin kiitanchchize oochchize bazita turo aazikaaya.
ACT 12:10 Kiitanchchizen Phexiroosan tiinon lam7intsa naagize zabiza aadhii katama kanggize birita furtsitigo yellida. Furtsita unttis fa faas erii bugunttida. Un kezii fettii ogera hyanggodera kiitanchchize tiirikaayzin Phexiroosappa shaakkinttida.
ACT 12:11 Phexiroosas wozintta maaqqin, «Tana Laatstsi fa Kiitanchchiza dakkii, Heroodisa kushtippan naagii bettide Ayhude asunts ubbappa ashshidanno hyatte turo erida» yagayda.
ACT 12:12 E yinno akaakide wode gaama asuntsi wolla shiiqii Xooz woossize besite, Marqqoosa gaaze Wahannisa intta Mayrami kara qitida.
ACT 12:13 Ize bale eqqii xeegida. Fettii Rooda ga7inttize arita furtsito bugodes yi7ida.
ACT 12:14 Rooda Phexiroosa qaala maaqqidanno eride wode ufayssar kumii bale bugikaayzin suub woxxii hyanggi, «Phexiroosa bale eqqida» yaga7i asuntsis ohida.
ACT 12:15 Asuntsi iigo, «Ne zhaashtane!» yagayda. Rooda Phexiroosa maaqqidanno geeshi ohida. Un, «Ye E kiitanchcho» yagayda.
ACT 12:16 Yezin Phexiroosa bale eqqii xeegii ashshanxin asuntsi furtsito bugii eza bi7i gaama qoppida.
ACT 12:17 Yezin un si77i gawude gaar Phexiroosa fa kushite mallii Laatstsi achi keetstsappa eza wayzi kessezako unttis qonccizi ohi, «Hyanno Yayqoobasin ammanze asuntsis ohote» ga7i izip kezii melle bessa qitida.
ACT 12:18 Sa7a wonttize wode «Phexiroosa aba qitido?» ga7i wottaddaruntsi wol gidda gaama kacinttida.
ACT 12:19 Heroodisa Phexiroosa koyzin, E dhabide wode naagizuntsana qurii, unttana wodhode gaar kiittida. Yinnippa suuba, Heroodisa Yihudappa Qisaariya wodhdhii ize eerats wode bettida.
ACT 12:20 Heroodisa Xiroosa asuntsallan Sidoona asuntsalla gaama kaccida. Un wolla fettilla yi7i kaat moorinna Bilasxoosa maadinttode gaara woossii yee7e ga7izii faas cima mahi giigodes Heroodisago hyanggida. Un gadita katstsa kaatize gadeppa denggane yeshsha.
ACT 12:21 Heroodisa shuuminttide wode fa ka7itumo afultto ma77i, araatalla bettii asuntsis ohida.
ACT 12:22 Asuntsi, «Yinna Xoozze qaala, as qaala baaya» yaga7i uukkida.
ACT 12:23 Heroodisa Xooz bonchchikaayze gisho iira Laatstse kiitanchcho eza guuddin zaqilara mu7intti hyayqqida.
ACT 12:24 Yezin Xoozze qaala dicciteran dalggitera hyanggida.
ACT 12:25 Barnnabaasan Sawulan fa oochito faaddii Marqqoosa gaaze Wahannisa faara ekkii Yerusalaamep maaqqida.
ACT 13:1 Anxookiya yeze woosa keetstsa nabuntsin asttamaaruntsin yene. Un Barnnabaasa, Kartsi ga7inttize Simoona, Qereenappa yi7ide Lukiyosa, Kaat Heroodisara diccide Minaahenen Saawulan.
ACT 13:2 Un Laatstsi goynoderan xoomodera Geeshi Ayyaana, «Taanii xeegide oochitis Barnnabaasan Sawulan taas shaakkote» yagayda.
ACT 13:3 Yinnii gisho, un xoomidaanippan woossidannippa maaqqii fa kushito unttalla gaddii dakkida.
ACT 13:4 Yinnii gisho, Geeshi Ayyaana unttana kiittida. Selewuqe hyanggida; iippa markkabe gidda gelii Qoophiroosa hyaatsara teqinttide sa7a qitida.
ACT 13:5 Un Silmmaana yellii Ayhude woosa keetstsa Xoozze qaala ohida. Wahannisa maadditera unttara yene.
ACT 13:6 Un Qoophiroosa hyaatsara teqinttide sa7a aadhii Phaafu yellize wode fettii worddo nabe Bar-Yesuusa gaaze Ayhude maro denggida.
ACT 13:7 Ye marize worzha ahize Sarggiyoosa Phawuloosa gaaze qofara yeze atstsera yene. Sarggiyoosa Phawuloosa Barnnabaasan Sawulan faago xeegii Xoozze qaala si7odes koyda.
ACT 13:8 Yezin Girike doonara marizay suntsitan «Elmmaasa» ga7inttane. E gade ahize ammanaame gaar kayodes koyi Barnnabaasan Phawuloosan ixxida.
ACT 13:9 Yezin Phawuloosa gaaze Saawula Geeshi Ayyaanara kumii marizaya dakkii bi7i,
ACT 13:10 «Naate, Xalahe na7ayo, iitatitsi ubba kumidayo, xillotitsi ubbas morkkizayo, luule Laatstse ogito mirqqizanno ashshoso?
ACT 13:11 Yikke, hyatte Laatstse kushe neella yene. Ne qooqe maaqqada; eerats wodes awa foo7o ba7aama» yagayda. Iira qayqayon dhuman E aafto goozin, fa kushito aykkii kaalitsize as koyitera wutida.
ACT 13:12 Gade ahize yinno bi7ide wode Laatstse baz tamaarssizanne gaama qoppii ammanida.
ACT 13:13 Phawuloosan eera yezuntsi Phaafuppa denddii, Phinfiliya yeze Phergge markkabera qitida. Wahannisa unttappa shaakkintti Yerusalaame maaqqida.
ACT 13:14 Yezin un Pherggeppa aadhii Phisidiya yeze Anxookiya yellida. Sambbata wode Ayhude woosa keetstsa gelii bettida.
ACT 13:15 Muse higgiton nabunts maxaaftan nabbabinttidannippa maaqqii Ayhude woosa Keetstsi hyalaquntsi, «Nu ishuntso, asi mintsitsize qaala yinttis yezako asuntsis ohoyate» ga7i unttago kiittida.
ACT 13:16 Phawuloosa denddii eqqii fa kushtira mallitera, «Isra7eele asuntsis, mahi Xooz goynize Ayhude maaqqoosse asuntso, si7ote.
ACT 13:17 Hyantsi Isra7eele asunts Xoozze, nu mayzuntsana doorida. Gibxxe sa7a zaqqotitsa un yessadera, unttana gaantsi fa damma wolqqara Gibxxe sa7appa unttana kessida.
ACT 13:18 Akko baayze sa7a oyttam bere gaar unttana dandda7ida.
ACT 13:19 Kanaane sa7a Ayhude maaqqoosse laappun ka7itumo kayi un gadito fa asuntsana laattizida.
ACT 13:20 Yinna ubba hyanidannippa oyddii xeet ichintam bere maaqqida. Yinnippa maaqqii Saamu7eela wode yellodes ahize daynna unttis inggida.
ACT 13:21 Yinnippa maaqqii, un faas kaati inggode gaar woossin, Xoozii Biniyame kochchappa Qiise na7a, Saawula oyttam bere ka7itode gaar unttis inggida.
ACT 13:22 Xoozii Saawula shaaridannippa maaqqii unttalla Dawute ka7itsida. Xoozii Dawutebaz markkidhite, ‹Ta wozintti gaar maaqqidaya ta qoftto ubba oochchiza Issey na7a Dawute denggida› gayda.
ACT 13:23 «Xoozii, taanii Dawute kochchappa Isra7eele asuntsana ufayssiza ko7oda gaydanni gaar Yesuusa ki7ida.
ACT 13:24 Yesuusa yo7odannippa tiino Isra7eele asuntsi ubba fa nagarttippa maaqqii xammaqinttode gaar Wahannisa qaala ohida.
ACT 13:25 Mahi Wahannisa fa oochchito folodes yi7ite asuntsago, ‹Tana oona ga7i qoppete? Taanii yin naagize Kiristtoosa baaya, yezin ta E caamma billodes taas beezoosse taappa suubite ye7ine› gayda.
ACT 13:26 «Ishuntso, Abrahama kochchuntso, mahi hyanne Ayhude maaqqikaayzara Xoozis zhashtizuntso, hyanna ashshize qaaltta nuus kiitinttida.
ACT 13:27 Akkos gayko, Yerusalaame yeze asuntsin un hyalaquntsi Yesuusa erikaaya. Sambbata ubbanne nabbabinttize nabunts qaaltto tiirikaayze gisho ezalla firddi nabuntsi ohide qaaltto folida.
ACT 13:28 Yesuusa wodhissades fettii miknaaten benttaanxin Philaaxoosa eza wodhodes inggode gaar woossida.
ACT 13:29 Un Yesuusa baz Geeshi Maxaafite xaafinttidanno ubba folide wode masqalappa eza ketstsii moogida.
ACT 13:30 Yezin Xoozii hyayqoppa Yesuusa dentsida.
ACT 13:31 Yinnippa maaqqii, E faara Galilappa Yerusalaame yi7iduntsis gaama qamma benttida. Un hyatte E baz asuntsis markkidhane.
ACT 13:32 «Xoozii nu aduntsis inggoda gayde Wonggele nuunii yinttis ohine.
ACT 13:33 Dawute fa Mazmure Maxaafite lam7intsa zofantte, « ‹Neenii, ta Na7aya, ta hyayno nena yelida› ga7intti xaafinttide Yesuusa, Xoozii hyayqoppa dentsii nu mayzuntsis inggoda gaydanno nuus un na7untsis folida.
ACT 13:34 E wooqaame gaar Xoozii hyayqoppa eza dentsite erisodes, « ‹Taanii Dawutes inggoda gayde ammaninttide geeshi anjjo yinttis inggoda› yaga7i ohida.
ACT 13:35 «Yinnii gisho, Mazmure Maxaafite melle bessa mahi, « ‹Ne Geeshize ahito wooqqizoos› gayda.
ACT 13:36 «Dawute fa wode Xoozze qoftto folidannippa maaqqii hyayqqii fa aduntsara mooginttii wooqqida.
ACT 13:37 Yezin Xoozii hyayqoppa dentsiday wooqqikaaya.
ACT 13:38 «Yinnii gisho, ta ishuntso, nagara ashshize Yesuusa zalara tiinidhdhii yinttis ohinttidanno erote. Muse higgita nagarappa xillissades dandda7oos.
ACT 13:39 Yezin Yesuusa ammanze ubbuntsi nagarappa xillane.
ACT 13:40 Yinnii gisho, nabuntsi gaydanna yinttana yellaame fana naaginttote.
ACT 13:41 « ‹Xoozii gaydebaz leqqizuntso! Bo7ote! Gaama qoppote! Dhabote! Ooden ohin, yin ammanoose oocha ta yin wodite oochchoda› » yagayda.
ACT 13:42 Phawuloosan Barnnabaasan Ayhude woosa keetstsappa kessadera, kaallize Sambbata yinno gujjii ohode gaar asuntsi unttana woossida.
ACT 13:43 Shiiqita lanttidannippa maaqqii gaama Ayhuduntsin Ayhudunts ammantte gelii Xooz goynize gaamuntsi Phawuloosan Barnnabaasan kaallida. Ammaniduntsii Xoozze aadho keehatitsite mintstsii yessade gaar unttana zorida.
ACT 13:44 Lam7intsa Sambbata katama yeze asuntsappa attide baaya yagawude wontsis Xoozze qaala si7odes shiiqida.
ACT 13:45 Yezin Ayhuduntsi gaama asuntsana be7eze wode Phawuloosa antsinttii E ohito ixxii eza cazhida.
ACT 13:46 Phawuloosan Barnnabaasan zhashtikaayzara, «Xoozze qaaltta tiinidhdhii yinttis ohinttodes beezane. Yezin yin qaala ixxii medhina de7o ekkodes nuus beezoos ga7i yin, yin ommite firddide gisho yikke nuunii Ayhude maaqqoosuntsago maaqqada.
ACT 13:47 Akkos gayko Laatstsi, « ‹Alame kumutsita ne baggara attode gaar, ta nena Ayhude maaqqoosse asuntsis foo7o mahida› ga7i nuna kiittida» gayda.
ACT 13:48 Ayhude maaqqoosuntsi yinno si7ide wode ufaytti Xoozze qaala bonchchida. Mahi medhina de7oos doorinttide ubba ammanida.
ACT 13:49 Laatstse qaaltta yinna sa7ito ubba yellida.
ACT 13:50 Yezin Ayhuduntsi, Ayhude maaqqoosse Xooz goynize bonchchinttide maachuntsanan katama yeze damma asuntsana Phawuloosallan Barnnabaasallan dentsitsida. Yentsi asuntsi unttana bay7e aykkii fa sa7itippa kessida.
ACT 13:51 Yezin Phawuloosaran Barnnabaasaran ixxizuntsis malla maaqqade gaar fa tohitippa xura fixxii Iqooniyone katama qitida.
ACT 13:52 Mahi Anxookiya yeze ammanzuntsi Geeshi Ayyaanaran ufayssara kumida.
ACT 14:1 Kasennigaara, Phawuloosan Barnnabaasan Iqooniyonen Ayhudunts woosa keetstsa gelii gaama Ayhuduntsin Ayhude maaqqoosuntsi ammanode wodes qaala ohida.
ACT 14:2 Yezin ammanikaayze Ayhuduntsi, Ayhude maaqqoosutsi wozintto laammii ishuntsalla dentsitsida.
ACT 14:3 Hawaaruntsi ize gaama wode gam77ida. Un zhashtikaayzara Laatstse baz ohida. Laatstsii mallan kille baz un oochchode gaar unttis adetits wolqqa inggi fa aadho keehatitsi qaaltta turo maaqqizanno beezida.
ACT 14:4 Yezin yentsi katama asuntsi shaakkintti, baggita Ayhuduntsara baggita mahi Hawaaruntsara maaqqida.
ACT 14:5 Ayhude maaqqoosuntsin Ayhuduntsin fa hyalaquntsara wolla maaqqii hawaaruntsana qohodesin shuchchara dhogodes koyda.
ACT 14:6 Hawaaruntsi yinno erii, Lisxiran Derbbe ga7inttize Liqaa7oniya katamuntsi giddan un guta yeze sa7a aachinttida.
ACT 14:7 Ize Wonggele ohida.
ACT 14:8 Yelinttidannippa aykkii lam77i tohita wobbin yedhdhii eroosse fettii asi Lisxira yene.
ACT 14:9 Ye atstsay Phawuloosa ohodera bettii si7ine. Phawuloosa eza dakkii be7ize wode faxodes ees ammano yezanno bi7i,
ACT 14:10 fa qaaltto dhoqi yiizii, «Moolii ne tohitira eqqo» yagayda. Yeezin, doollii denddii eqqii yedhdhe aykkida.
ACT 14:11 Phawuloosa oochchidanno asuntsi bi7i fa qaaltto dhoqi yiizii Liqaa7oniya doonara, «Eequntsi asi aazii nuugo wodhdhida» yagayda.
ACT 14:12 Barnnabaasa, «Diya» ga7i, Phawuloosa ohize waannize gisho eza, «Hermmeene» ga7i suntsida.
ACT 14:13 Katamappa gaxa yeze Diya goyno keetstsa kahinzen asuntsi kormman bonchcho fudhe hawaaruntsis zharshodes koyi katama furtsa ki7ida.
ACT 14:14 Yezin Barnnabaasan Phawuloosan yinno si7eze wode un oochchodes qoppidanno ixxii fa ma7ito feedhida. Asunts gidda woxxii gelii,
ACT 14:15 fa qaaltto dhoqi yiizii, «Asuntso, hyanno akkos oochchete? Nuunin yin fana asi. Hyanna fatstsoosse bazitippa salon sa7an, abba un gidda yeze ubbabazito medhdhide de7o Xoozzego yin maaqqade gaar yinttis nuunii Wonggele ohine.
ACT 14:16 E zaga asuntsana fa ogito yedhdhade gaar dakkii ashshida.
ACT 14:17 Yezin ira saloppa bukkizida, katstsan woder woder inggida, katstsa inggi yinttana gaama ufayssida, yeyzi yinttis lo77o baz oochchii faas markka dhabsikaaya» yagayda.
ACT 14:18 Hawaaruntsi yinno ga7i faas asuntsi zharshaame gaar waayi kayda.
ACT 14:19 Anxookiyappan Iqooniyoneppan yi7ide Ayhuduntsi, asuntsana fa zala mahi shuchchara Phawuloosa dhogida. Unttis E hyayqqide gaar aazin katamappa gaxa gochchii kanggi olida.
ACT 14:20 Yezin ammanzuntsi yi7i, E kale wutii eqqezin E denddii katama gelida. Wonttisti wode Barnnabaasara wolla Darbbe qitida.
ACT 14:21 Un Darbbe katama Wonggele ohi gaamuntsana ammanzuntsana mahidannip suuba Lisxira, Iqooniyonen Phisidiya Anxookiya maaqqida.
ACT 14:22 Ize ammanzuntsi ammanora miinggi yessade gaar zorii, «Xoozze ka7itumo gelodes nuunii gaama madha ekkodes beezane» yaga7i tamaarssida.
ACT 14:23 Mahi woosa keetstsis ommite ommite cimuntsana doorida. Xoomidannippan woossidannippa maaqqii un ammanize Laatstses un hyadarito inggidda.
ACT 14:24 Phisidiya sa7a kantsii aadhii Phinfiliya qitida.
ACT 14:25 Pherggen qaala ohidannippa maaqqii Axaaliya qitida.
ACT 14:26 Iippa un fa folide oochitis Xoozze aadho keehatitsitis unttis hyadara inggide Anxookiya markkabera maaqqida.
ACT 14:27 Anxookiya yelide wode woosa keetstsa asuntsana shiishii Xoozii unttara oochchide oochito ubba Ayhude maaqqoosse asuntsi ammanode gaar unttis wayzi furtsi bugezako ohida.
ACT 14:28 Ezin ammanzuntsara gaama wode gam77ida.
ACT 15:1 Fettii fettii asuntsi Yihudappa Anxookiya hyanggi, «Muse wogiti gaar yin garrazinttanxiko attodes dandda7oos» ga7i ammanzuntsana tamaarsse aykkida.
ACT 15:2 Yinna Phawuloosan Barnnabaasan unttara gaama lallode gaaran kacinttode gaar yiizida. Yinnii gisho, Anxookiya yeze fettii fettii asuntsi Phawuloosaran Barnnabaasara Yerusalaame hyanggi Hawaaruntsara cimuntsara yellintti yinna ohito billode gaar qofa accinttida.
ACT 15:3 Woosa keetsita unttana kiittin qitida. Un Finqeran Samaarera aadhittera Ayhude maaqqoosuntsi Xoozago wayzi maaqqezako ohida. Yinna ammanzuntsana ubba gaama ufayssida.
ACT 15:4 Un Yerusalaame yellide wode woosa keetsita, Hawaaruntsin cimuntsi unttana mokkida. Xoozii unttara oochchidanno ubba ohida.
ACT 15:5 Yezin Farisaawunts baggappa ammanide fettii fettii asuntsi denddii eqqii, «Ayhude maaqqoosse ammanize asuntsi garrazinttodesin Muse higgito naagodes beezane» yagayda.
ACT 15:6 Hawaaruntsin cimuntsi yinno zorinttodes shiiqida.
ACT 15:7 Gaama ohinttidannippa maaqqii, Phexiroosa denddii eqqii, «Ta ishuntso, Ayhude maaqqoosuntsi Wonggele qaala ta doonappa si7i ammanode gaar tiinidhii tana Xoozii yin giddappa dooridanno yin erane.
ACT 15:8 As wozina erize Xoozze Geeshi Ayyaana nuus inggidannigaar unttisin inggi turizida.
ACT 15:9 Ammanora un wozintto geeshide gisho nu giddan un gidda shaako gaddikaaya.
ACT 15:10 Yinnii gisho, nu aduntsin nuunii tookkodes dandda7oos qambbara ammanzuntsi geetalla gaddii hyatte akkos Xooz fattanete?
ACT 15:11 Laatstse Yesuus aadho keehatitsite un attidanni gaara nuunin attidanno ammanane» yagayda.
ACT 15:12 Asuntsi si77i ga7i, Barnnabaasan Phawuloosa Ayhude maaqqoosse asunts gidda un baggara Xoozii oochchide mallan kille bazi ubba ohodera si7ine.
ACT 15:13 Un ohi hyaasidannippa maaqqii Yayqooba, «Ishuntso, ta gaazanno si7ote.
ACT 15:14 Xoozii Ayhude maaqqoosuntsi gidda fa fa suntsito xeegize worzha doorodes koyi unttana tiino wayzi qoppezako Simoona ohida.
ACT 15:15 Nabunts qaaltta hyannira giigane. Geeshi Maxaafite,
ACT 15:16 « ‹Hyannippa suuba, ta maaqqada, Woddide Dawute keetsito keexxoda. Wul7inttide keetsiton mahi essoda.
ACT 15:17 Attide asuntsi ubba taago ye7oda, ta xeegide Ayhude maaqqoosse asuntsi ubba tana koyoda. Zagappa aykkii yinna erinttode fana yiizide Laatstse, ohine› yagayda.
ACT 15:19 «Yinnii gisho, ta qoftta Xoozago maaqqize Ayhude maaqqoosuntsana nuunii waaytsosako lo77o.
ACT 15:20 Yezin un eeqas zharshinttii tunidebaz ma7aame gaar, olalaame gaar, bawuta ma7aame gaaran suutsi uzhaame gaaran ma7aame gaar unttis nuunii dabddaabbe xaafodes beezane.
ACT 15:21 Muse higge zagappa aykkii Sambbata Sambbata Ayhude woosa keetstsa nabbabinttii katama ubba sabbakinttane» yagayda.
ACT 15:22 Yinnippa maaqqii, hawaaruntsin cimuntsi woosa keetstsa as ubbuntsara fettilla fa gidda fa eerats asuntsana doorii Phawuloosaran Barnnabaasara Anxookiya dakkodes qofa accida. Gaama erinttide kaalitsizuntsana Barssabaasa ga7inttize Yihudan Sillaasen doorida.
ACT 15:23 Hyannigaara ga7intti dabddaabbe unttalla dakkida: «Nu hawaaruntsin cimuntsi yin ishuntsi, Anxookiya, Sooriya Kilqiya yeze Ayhude maaqqoosse ishuntsis nu sarotits kiittida.
ACT 15:24 «Nuunii kiittikaayze asuntsi nu giddappa hyanggi, ‹Yin garrazinttodesin higgito naagodes beezane› ga7i, yinttana waaytsidannon zhilizidanno si7ida.
ACT 15:25 Nuunii kadhize Barnnabaasan Phawuloosa doorinttide asuntsara wolla yinttago dakkodes fettii wozinara nu qoftto accida.
ACT 15:26 Un nu Laatstse Yesuus Kiristtoosa gisho fa de7ito aatsii inggida.
ACT 15:27 Yinnii gisho, nu xaafidanno un fa doonara gujjii yinttis ohode fana Yihudan Sillaasen kiittida.
ACT 15:28 «Hyanna koshshizuntsap attin melle toofo yinttana toossame gaar nuunin Geeshi Ayyaana ohito accida.
ACT 15:29 Eeqas zharshinttii tunidebaz mu7ippete, suutsi uzhippete, bawuta mu7ippete, olalippete. Hyantsi ubbappa yin, yin ommito naagiko lo77o baz oochchane. Lo77o yezote» yagayda.
ACT 15:30 Yinnii gisho, kiitinttiduntsi moyzinttii Anxookiya qitii ammanze asuntsana shiishii, dabddaabbiza inggidda.
ACT 15:31 Un ye mintsitsize dabddaabbiza nabbabide wode ufayttida.
ACT 15:32 Mahi Yihudan Sillaasen fa ommite nabuntsana maaqqide gisho ammanzuntsana loytsii zorii mintsitsida.
ACT 15:33 Un Anxookiya eeratsi wode bettidannippa suuba ammanze ishuntsi loytsi moyzin fana kiittezuntsago maaqqida.
ACT 15:34 [Yezin Sillaasen ize attodes koyda.]
ACT 15:35 Mahi Phawuloosan Barnnabaasan melle gaama asuntsara wolla Laatstse qaala tamaarssitera Wonggele ohitera Anxookiya gam77ida.
ACT 15:36 Eerats qammappa suuba Phawuloosa Barnnabaasago, «Nu Laatstse qaala ohide katamite ubba ammanizuntsi wayzi yezako suuba maaqqitera be7ada» yagayda.
ACT 15:37 Barnnabaasa Marqqoosa ga7inttize Wahannisa faara hyammade fana koyda.
ACT 15:38 Yezin Phawuloosa Marqqoosa faara hyammade fana koykaaya. Akkos gayko, E Phinfiliya shaakkintti unttara oochchodes hyanggikaaya.
ACT 15:39 Un gidda iita kachchi kezin fetay fetayppa shaakkinttida. Barnnabaasa Marqqoosa ekkii markkabera Qoophiroosa qitida.
ACT 15:40 Yezin Phawuloosa Sillaase doorida; ammanzuntsi Phawuloosa Xoozze aadho keehatitsi hyadarito inggidannippa maaqqii E kezii qitida.
ACT 15:41 Yeyzi, woosa keetstsi mintsitsitera Sooriyaran Kilqiyaran wutida.
ACT 16:1 Phawuloosa Darbben Lisxiran qitida. Ize Ximotiyoosa gaaze ammanize asi yene. E intta ammanze Ayhude maacho, E aday Girike asi.
ACT 16:2 Lisxiran Iqooniyone yeze ammanzuntsi Ximotiyoosa baz loytsii markkidhida.
ACT 16:3 Phawuloosa Ximotiyoosa faara ekkodes koyi, E aday Girike asi maaqqidanno yinna besite yeze Ayhude ubbuntsi erize gisho eza garrazida.
ACT 16:4 Un katamara aadhitter Yerusalaame yeze hawaaruntsin cimuntsin accide qoftto ammanzuntsi naagode gaar unttis ohitera aadhida.
ACT 16:5 Yinnii gisho, woosa keetsita ammanora miinggite, faydoran qammite qammite gaanggitter hyanggida.
ACT 16:6 Isiya gidda qaala ohaame gaar Geeshi Ayyaana unttana kayde gisho Phirggeran Galaatiya sa7ara aadhida.
ACT 16:7 Un Miisiya gaxa yellide wode Bitiiniya qitodes qoppida yeshsha. Yezin Yesuusa Ayyaana unttana kayda.
ACT 16:8 Yinnii gisho, un Miisiya kalera aadhitera Xiro7aada wodhdhida.
ACT 16:9 Phawuloosa qamma qonccitsara fettii Maqedooniya asi faago, «Maqedooniya fiinggi nuna maaddoya» ga7i eqqii woossodera bi7ida.
ACT 16:10 Qonccitsi E bi7idannippa maaqqii nu Maqedooniya qitodes koyda. Yinnan, Wonggele ize yeze asuntsis ohodes Xoozii nuna xeegida aazida.
ACT 16:11 Xiro7aadappa denddii markkabe gidda gelii Samotiraaqe hyanggide, wonttisti wode Naaphule hyanggida.
ACT 16:12 Izippa denddii Maqedooniya sa7a yeze Filphisiyusa ga7inttize worada katama hyanggida. Mahi Filphisiyusa Roomuntsi ahize katama. Nu yinna katamite eeratsi wode bettida.
ACT 16:13 Sambbata wode katamappa gaxa borkka doona Ayhuduntsi Xoozze woossize bessi yezanno qoppii ize hyanggida. Yinna besite shiiqide maachuntsis qaala ohida.
ACT 16:14 Nuna si7ize asuntsappa fettii Liidiya ga7inttize Tiyaxiroone katamappa yi7ide, Xooz ammanze zoqo ma7o zal77ize, maachita yene. Phawuloosa ohizanno iza si7ode gaar Laatstsii I wozintto bugida.
ACT 16:15 Liidiya fa kara asuntsara wolla xammaqinttidannippa maaqqii nuugo, «Yin tana Laatstsa turo ammanida gayko ta kara yi7i shemppote» ga7i mintsii woossida.
ACT 16:16 Nu Xooz woossize besite hyanggodera iita ayyaana iilla afa yezii maridhdhize fettii wudur arita nuura yellinttida. Iza maridhdhii gaama bira fa laatstsuntsis ke7ine.
ACT 16:17 Phawuloosan nunan kaallii, «Hyantses Ubbappa kattara Xoozze aruntsana! Un yin attode ogito ohizuntsana» ga7i uukkida.
ACT 16:18 Ubba wode yinnii gaar gaane. Yezin Phawuloosa zhilidhdhi suub maaqqii, ye ayyaanza, «Yesuus Kiristtoosa suntsite iippa kezo» ga7i kiittida. Iira iita ayyaanze iippa kezida.
ACT 16:19 Yezin I laatstsuntsi faas bira denggize ogita dhabidanno bi7i, Phawuloosan Sillaasen aykkii, firdda keetstsa daynnuntsi tiino gochchii kanggida.
ACT 16:20 Daynnuntsi tiino unttana kanggi, «Hyantses Ayhude asi maaqqii nu katama asuntsana gaama waaytstsane.
ACT 16:21 Nu Roome gade asuntsi ekkodesin oochchodes woga maaqqoosse baz tamaarssane» gayda.
ACT 16:22 Asuntsi fettii zala maaqqii, Phawuloosallan Sillaaselan denddida. Daynnuntsi un ma7ito gaarii gufer unttana guuddade fana kiittida.
ACT 16:23 Unttana gaama hyadhdhidannippa suuba achi keetstsa geltsida. Achi keetstsito kafizay unttana mintsii kafode gaar kiittida.
ACT 16:24 Achi keetstsito kafize yinna kiitto ekkii, Phawuloosan Sillaasen achi keetstsitis qol7a geltsida. Un tohito dutstsara accida.
ACT 16:25 Yezin qamma bilahe maaqqize wode Phawuloosaran Sillaaseran woossitteran mazmure yexxitteran Xooz galatane. Achi keetstsite yeze melle asuntsin un gaazanno si7ine.
ACT 16:26 Qoppikaayzin achi keetsiti sa7ita en7inttode wontsis sa7a en7ida. Yinna saatte furtsita ubba bugunttii attida; acinttide asuntsi ubbuntsi santsalaata bilinttii wodhdhida.
ACT 16:27 Achi keetstsito kafize genttoppa barkkide wode achi keetsiti furtsita ubba bugunttidanno bi7i acinttide asuntsi kessii ekkii qitide gaar aazin fana wodhodes mashsha ekkida.
ACT 16:28 Yezin Phawuloosa fa qaaltto dhoqi yiizii «Nu ubbanna hyanne yeze gisho ne nena qohippe» gayda.
ACT 16:29 Achi keetstsito kafize xomppe woossii ekkii ellisii gidda woxxida. Goqitera Phawuloosa tiinon Sillaase tiino zuggida.
ACT 16:30 Unttana bale kessii, «Ta laatstsuntso, ta attodes akko oochchodes beeze?» gayda.
ACT 16:31 Phawuloosaran Sillaasera eego, «Laatstsi Yesuus Kiristtoosa ammano; neeran ne kara asuntsaran attoda» gayda.
ACT 16:32 Un eesin E kara yeze ubbuntsis Laatstse qaala ohida.
ACT 16:33 Qamma yinna saatte achi keetsito kafize unttana kanggi un hyarggize bessito meeccida. Ellisii fa kara as ubbuntsara xammaqinttida.
ACT 16:34 Phawuloosan Sillaasen fa kara kanggi unttis katstsa aatstsida. E fa kara asi ubbuntsara Xooz ammanide gisho ufayttida.
ACT 16:35 Sa7ita wonttin daynnuntsi, «Yentsi asuntsana billo» yaga7i foolisuntsana eego kiittida.
ACT 16:36 Achi keetsito kafize, «Yin bilinttode gaar daynnuntsi kiittida. Yikke, kezii saro qitote» yaga7i yinna kiitto Phawuloosas ohida.
ACT 16:37 Yezin Phawuloosa yentsi foolisuntsago, «Nu Roome asi maaqqadera un nuna firdda baytsi as tiino hyadhdhii, achi keetstsa olida. Hyatte nuna aachintti kezii qito gaane? Hyanoos, un fa ommitis yi7i nuna kesso» gayda.
ACT 16:38 Foolisuntsi daynnuntsis yinno ohin, Phawuloosaran Sillaaseran Roome sa7a asi maaqqidanno si7ide wode zhashtida.
ACT 16:39 Yinnii gisho, daynnuntsi yi7i unttago, Nu yinttana qohida yaga7i maarotitsi oocida. Achi keetsitippa bale unttana kessii, katamappa kezii qitode gaar woossida.
ACT 16:40 Phawuloosaran Sillaaseran achi keetsitippa kezii Liidiya kara hyanggida. Ize ammanzuntsara yellintti unttana mintsitsii kezii qitida.
ACT 17:1 Phawuloosara Sillaaseran Amfipholisaran Apholoniyara aadhii Teselonqe qitida. Ize Ayhude woosa keetstsi yene.
ACT 17:2 Phawuloosa zaganni gaara ize gelida. Ize hyaydzdzii sambbata Xoozze qaalappa asuntsis ohida.
ACT 17:3 Kiristtoosa madha ekkodesin hyayqoppa denddodesin beezanno unttis geeshi ohitera, «Yesuusa hyay ta yinttis ohizay Kiristtoosa» yagayda.
ACT 17:4 Unttappa fete fete ohidanna turo maaqqidanno ekkii Phawuloosaran Sillaasera wolla fetto maaqqida. Yinnii fana, Xooz goynize gaama Girike asuntsin gaama bonchchinttide maachuntsin unttara wolla maaqqida.
ACT 17:5 Yezin Ayhuduntsi ixxii fettii fettii oocha baayze iita asuntsana ogeppa shiishida. Katamito buqe aykkida; Phawuloosan Sillaasen asuntsis aatsii inggodes koyi Iyaasone keetstsito teqqida.
ACT 17:6 Phawuloosan Sillaasen unttis benttaanxin, Iyaasonen fettii fettii ammanzuntsana katama hyalaquntsago gochchii kanggi, «Hyantses sa7ito ubba buqizuntsi hyatte nuugo yi7ida.
ACT 17:7 Iyaasone unttana fa kara gaddida. Hyantses, ‹Yesuusa gaaze melle kaati yene› ga7i Qeesare kiitto ixxane» ga7i dhoqi gayde qaalara ohida.
ACT 17:8 Shiiqide asuntsin katama hyalaquntsi yinno si7i hyanodebaz dhabida.
ACT 17:9 Hyalaquntsi Iyaasonan melluntsana waaser billida.
ACT 17:10 Ammanzuntsi Phawuloosan Sillaasen qammara Beeriya dakkida. Beeriya yellii, Ayhude woosa keetstsa gelida.
ACT 17:11 Beeriya asuntsi Teselonqe asuntsappa aadhii wozina dalgga. Un qaaltto kumutsi wozinappa ekkida; Phawuloosa gaydanna turo maaqqidanno shaakkii erodes ubba wode Geeshi Maxaafe nabbabane.
ACT 17:12 Yinnii gisho, unttappa gaamuntsi, Girikuntsappa bonchchinttide gaama maachuntsin gaama dhiiratsuntsii ammanida.
ACT 17:13 Yezin Teselonqe yeze Ayhuduntsi Phawuloosa Xoozze qaala Beeriy giddan ohidanno si7ide wode Beeriya yi7i asuntsana buqida.
ACT 17:14 Yinnippa maaqqii, ammanzuntsi ellisii Phawuloosa abba kale dakkida. Yezin Sillaasen Ximotiyoosan Beeriya attida.
ACT 17:15 Phawuloosa moyzide asuntsi Ateena yeltsida. Yentsi asuntsi Sillaasen Ximotiyoosan faas dandda7inttide gaar ellisii faago ye7ode gaar Phawuloosa kiitteze kiitto ekkii Beeriya maaqqida.
ACT 17:16 Phawuloosa Ateena Sillaasen Ximotiyoosan kafittera, katama eeqa kumidanno bi7i zhilidhdhida.
ACT 17:17 Yinnii gisho, Ayhude woosa Keetsite Ayhuduntsaran Xooz goynize Ayhude maaqqoosse asuntsara mahi faara yellinttize asuntsara ubba wode gabe lallane.
ACT 17:18 Ephiqoroosan Isttoyke ga7inttize bagguntsappa fettii fettii eruntsi Phawuloosara wolla lallida. Unttappa fete fete, «Hyay canccize akko ohodes koye?» yagayda. Melluntsi Phawuloosa Yesuusan hyayqoppa denddo baz faas ohide gisho «Melle eequntsi baz ohiza aazane» yagayda.
ACT 17:19 Phawuloosa aykkii Aryoospaagosa gaaze shiiqo besite kanggi, «Hyanna ne tamaarssize kille bazita akko yezakon nuna eriso?
ACT 17:20 Akkos gayko, ne nuus kille baz ohine; yikke yinna akko yezakon nu erodes koyane» yagayda.
ACT 17:21 Ateena asuntsi ubbuntsin ize yeze zaqquntsi kille baz ohikaayzaran si7ikaayzaran feezhoos.
ACT 17:22 Phawuloosa Aryoospaagosa gidda shiiqide asuntsi tiino eqqii, «Ateena asuntso, yin eequntsis ubba baza gaama zhashtizanno ta bi7ida.
ACT 17:23 Taanii yin katamara wutittera yin goynize besite be7ize wode ‹Erinttoose Xoozzes› ga7intti xaafinttide zharsho bessito denggida. Hyanna yin erikaayzara goynizaya ta yinttis ohoda.
ACT 17:24 Sa7an sa7alla yeze ubbabazito medhdhide Xoozze, salon sa7a Laatstse, asi keexxide keetstsa yezoos.
ACT 17:25 E de7o, shemppon ubba baz as ubbas inggide gisho face yeze asi fana as maade koyoos.
ACT 17:26 Xoozii un yessade wodesin bessis wuzula inggida. Yinnippa as kochchi ubba fettii asappa medhdhii sa7a ubba gaddida.
ACT 17:27 E yinno oochchidanna asi eza koyode fanan qurichchi denggode fana. Maaqqikon E nuuppa hyaako baaya.
ACT 17:28 Yinttappa fettii fettii yexxizuntsi, ‹Nu E na7untsana› maaqqidanni fana, Nu E gidda faxa yene, en7inttane.
ACT 17:29 Yikke, nu Xoozze na7untsana maaqqide gisho ‹Xoozii as yiillatitsaran qofara worqqappa woy birappa woy shuchchappa oochinttidebaz aazane› ga7i qoppodes beezoos.
ACT 17:30 Yinnii gisho, Xoozii tiino wode asi erikaayzara oochchidanno ashshii aadhida, yezin hyatte ubba bessa yeze asi ubba nagarappa maaqqade gaar kiittane.
ACT 17:31 Akkos gayko, Xoozii fa dooride atstsera sa7alla yeze asi ubballa xillo firdda firddodes qamma giigizii gaddida. Eza hyayqoppa dentsii yinno as ubbas geeshida» gayda.
ACT 17:32 Unttappa fettii fettii asuntsi hyayqoppa denddebaz Phawuloosappa si7i, eza leqqida. Yezin melluntsi, «Nuunii yinno neeppa gujjii si7odes koyane» gayda.
ACT 17:33 Yinnii gisho, Phawuloosa un giddappa kezida.
ACT 17:34 Yezin fettii fettii dhiiratsuntsii Phawuloosara yellii ammanida. Un giddappa Aryoospaagosan shiiqite yeze Diyonasyoosa gaaze atstse, Damariso gaaze fettii maachitan melluntsin unttara yene.
ACT 18:1 Yinnippa suuba, Phawuloosa Ateenappa kezii, Qoronttoosa qitida.
ACT 18:2 Ize Aqiila gaaze Phanxoosa yelinttide fettii Ayhude as denggida. Ayhude asuntsana ubba Roomeppa kessade gaar kaati Qalawudiyoosa kiittide gisho eeratsi wodeppa tiino E fa machchitii Phirisqilara Xaaleppa yi7ida. Phawuloosa unttara yellinttodes hyanggida.
ACT 18:3 E oochita unttinnigaara dunkkaane sikke maaqqide gisho unttara bettii wolla oochchida.
ACT 18:4 Phawuloosa Sambbata ubba Ayhuduntsanan Girikuntsana ammantsodes Ayhude woosa Keetstsa miinggi ohine.
ACT 18:5 Sillaasen Ximotiyoosan Maqedooniyappa yi7ide wode Phawuloosa fa kumutsi wodito inggi Ayhuduntsis Yesuusa E, Kiristtoosa ga7i qaala ohida.
ACT 18:6 Yezin un Phawuloosa ixxii eza cazhin Phawuloosa fa ma7itippa xura tiqizi, «Yin gomtta yinttana yello; ta yinne yezoos. Yikkeppa suuba, ta Ayhude maaqqoosse asuntsago qitane» gayda.
ACT 18:7 Izip kezii Xooz goynize Titoos Yosxoosa gaaze atstse kara qitida. Yosxoosa keetsita Ayhude woosa Keetstsi kale yene.
ACT 18:8 Ayhude woosa Keetsiti hyalaqize Qarisphoosa fa kara asuntsi ubbuntsara Laatstsii ammanida. Qoronttoosa asuntsappa gaamuntsi Xooz qaala si7ide wode ammanii xammaqinttida.
ACT 18:9 Laatstsii fettii qamma Phawuloosas benttii, «Zhashtippe; oho, si77i gayppe.
ACT 18:10 Taanii neera yene. Taas hyanna katamite, gaama asi yeze gisho nena qohii iitabessa olode asi ooden baaya» gayda.
ACT 18:11 Yinnii gisho, Phawuloosa Xoozze qaala asuntsana tamaarssittera fettii beren izippun agina unttara bettida.
ACT 18:12 Gaaliyoosa Akkaya sa7a ahize wode Ayhuduntsi fettilla Phawuloosalla denddii firdda keetstsa eza kanggi,
ACT 18:13 «Hyay atstsay higge ixxii, asuntsi Xooz goynode gaar yiizane» gayda.
ACT 18:14 Phawuloosa ohodes yi7adera, Gaaliyoosa Ayhuduntsago, «Ayhuduntso, yinna iita oocha woy qohe maaqqiko ta yin baz dandda7i si7odes beezane.
ACT 18:15 Yezin qaalasin, suntsisin yin higgitisin yin lallizebaz maaqqiko yin, yinttis billote; yinno ta firddoos» gayda.
ACT 18:16 Yeyzi, unttana firdda keetstsappa bale kessida.
ACT 18:17 Yinnippa suuba, asuntsi ubba Ayhude woosa Keetstsa hyalaqiza Sostenisa aykkii firdda keetstsi tiino hyadhdhida. Yezin Gaaliyoosas yinna akkon aazikaaya.
ACT 18:18 Phawuloosa gaama wode Qoronttoosa gidda bettidanippa suuba ammanze asuntsana sarotsi, Phirisqiliran Aqiilara markkabera Sooriya qitida. Yezin E qitodannippa tiino faas qayinggidebaz yeze gisho Kinkkiriya katama fa ommito medinttida.
ACT 18:19 Un Efesoone yelide wode Phawuloosa Phirisqilan Aqiilan ize ashshida. Yezin faas Ayhude woosa keetstsa gelii Ayhuduntsara ohinttida.
ACT 18:20 Un faara gaama wode bettode gaar Phawuloosa woossida yezin E ixxida.
ACT 18:21 Unttappa shaakkinttiter; «Xoozii gayko yinttago maaqqii yo7oda» yaga7i Efesooneppa markkabera qitida.
ACT 18:22 Qisaariya yellide wode Yerusalaame hyanggi woosa keetstsa asuntsana saritstsidannippa suuba Anxookiya qitida.
ACT 18:23 Ize eeratsi wode gam77idannippa suuba ammanize asuntsana ubba mintsitsitera Galaatiyaran Phirggeran aadhida.
ACT 18:24 Iskkinddiriya yelinttide fettii Aphiloosa gaaze Ayhude asi Efesoone qitida. E ohe erize asin Xoozze qaala gaama erize asi.
ACT 18:25 E Laatstsii ogito tamaarii, ayyaanara eexii Yesuusa baz luule tamaarssane. Maaqqo yezin, Wahannisa xinqqate xalaala erane.
ACT 18:26 E Ayhude woosa Keetstsite zhashtikaayzara tamaarssane. Phirisqilan Aqiilan E ohizanno si7ide wode eza faara kara kanggi Xoozze ogito tiinositippa geeshi ees ohida.
ACT 18:27 Aphiloosa Akkaya qitodes koyin Efesoone yeze ammanize asuntsi E qoftto ekkii Akkaya yeze ammanzuntsi eza mokkode gaar unttis dabddaabbe xaafida. E ize yelide wode Xoozze aadho keehatitsiti baggara Yesuus Kiristtoosa ammaniduntsana gaama maaddida.
ACT 18:28 Akkos gayko, Yesuusa E Kiristtoosa maaqqizanno Ayhuduntsis Xoozze qaalappa qonccizi asunts tiino mintsii ohi unttana latstsida.
ACT 19:1 Aphiloosa Qoronttoosa yessadera, Phawuloosa wookka zalara aadhii Efesoone qitida. Izen fettii fettii ammanze asuntsana denggida.
ACT 19:2 Unttago, «Yin ammanide wode Geeshi Ayyaana ekkidate?» ga7i oocida. Un, «Ade, ekkikaaya; melle atto yezin, Geeshi Ayyaana yezannon si7ikaaya» gayda.
ACT 19:3 Phawuloosa unttago, «Yeezin, akkor xammaqinttidote?» gayda. Un, «Nuunii Wahannisa xinqate xammaqinttida» ga7i mahida.
ACT 19:4 Phawuloosa, «Wahannisa faappa suubar ye7ize Yesuus ammanode gaar asuntsis ohiter, nagarappa maaqqes koshshize xinqate xammaqinttida» gayda.
ACT 19:5 Un yinno si7ide wode Laatstse Yesuusa tamaare maaqqades xammaqinttida.
ACT 19:6 Phawuloosa fa kushito unttalla gaddize wode Geeshi Ayyaana unttalla wodhdhin, melle melle doonara wolla ohinttida; mahi tinbbite ohida.
ACT 19:7 Yinna besite taphpho lam77i maaqqize asuntsi yene.
ACT 19:8 Phawuloosa Ayhude woosa Keetstsa gelii, Xoozze ka7itumo baz zhashtikaayzara markkidhiter loytsii qoncciziter unttara hyaydzdzii agina yellodes gam7ida.
ACT 19:9 Yezin unttappa fete fete dhube maaqqii gaama asunts tiino Laatstse ogito cazhi ammananxii ixxida. Phawuloosa ammanzuntsana unttappa shagii ekkii Xiranoosa gaaze timirtte keetstsa ubba wode unttana tamaarssida.
ACT 19:10 Phawuloosa lam77i bere yellodes qaala ohida. Yinnii gisho, Isiya yeze asuntsi ubba, Ayhuduntsin Ayhude maaqqoosuntsi Laatstse qaala si7ida.
ACT 19:11 Xoozii Phawuloosa kushite damma kille baz oochchida.
ACT 19:12 Yinnii gisho, asuntsi E gallito bochchide maarabito woy ma7ito hyargganchchuntsis kanggane. Unttin faxane; tuna ayyaanuntsin unttappa kezane.
ACT 19:13 Tuna ayyaana kessitera wutize Ayhuduntsappa fete fete, «Phawuloosa sabbakize Yesuusa suntsite kezote ga7i yinttana kiittane» ga7i, tuna ayyaana aykkide asuntsalla Laatstse Yesuusa suntsito xeegida
ACT 19:14 Ayhude maaqqide Kahinunts hyalaqappa fettii Asqeewe gaaze atstses yinno oochchize laappun dhiiratsi na7unts yene.
ACT 19:15 Yezin tuna ayyaanze unttago, «Taanii Yesuusan erane Phawuloosa bazin erane, yezin yin oode?» yagayda.
ACT 19:16 Tuna ayyaanze aykkide atstse unttalla doollii wodhdhi, unttana hyarggizi, yinna keetsitippa kallo woxxi dhabode wontsis wolqqidhdhida.
ACT 19:17 Efesoone yeze Ayhuduntsin Ayhude maaqqoosuntsi ubba yinno si7i gaama zhashtida. Laatstsii Yesuusa suntsita gaama bonchchinttida.
ACT 19:18 Ammanzuntsappa gaamuntsi fa oochchide iita oochito buuxitera qoncce ohiter yene.
ACT 19:19 Bitizuntsappa gaamuntsi fa maxaafito shiishii as ubba tiino michchida. Yinna maxaafti waagita ichintam mukul shuchchi bira santime maaqqida.
ACT 19:20 Yinnii gaar yi7i Xoozze qaala wolqqar dicciteran dalggitter qitida.
ACT 19:21 Yinna folinttidanippa suuba Phawuloosa, «Taanii Yerusalaame qitii maaqqii Roomen hyanggodes beezane» ga7i Maqedooniyaran Akkayaran aadhii Yerusalaame hyanggodes qofa accida.
ACT 19:22 Mahi fana maaddizuntsappa lam77untsana Ximotiyoosan Erasxoosa Maqedooniya kiittii, faas Isiya gidda eerats wode gam7ida.
ACT 19:23 Ye wode Laatstse ogiti gisho Efesoone gidda damma kachchi kezida.
ACT 19:24 Fettii bira qoxxize Dimexiroosa gaaze atstse Arxemiisa eeqa keetstsa misile birappa medhdhii gaama tirfe dinggizanne.
ACT 19:25 Yinnii gisho, yinnii fana oocha oochchizuntsana fettilla shiishii, «Asuntso, nu duretitsita hyanna oochite maaqqidanno yin erane.
ACT 19:26 Hyay Phawuloosa, ‹As kushe medhinttide eequntsana baane› ga7i, Efesoonen eeratsi sa7ap attin kumutsi Isiya ubba yeze gaama asuntsana ohi ammantsidannon balitsidannon yin bi7ida si7ida.
ACT 19:27 Madha maaqqidanna, nu oochita leqqinttizanno xalaala maaqqikaayzin Isiya sa7a ubba yeze asi goynize damma eeqa Arxemiisa keetsita bonchchinttikaayzar attodanna I dammatitsita gol7odanno» gayda.
ACT 19:28 Asuntsi yinno si7eze wode zhilidhdhi, «Efesoone Arxemiisa damma» ga7i uukkida.
ACT 19:29 Yinna uufita katama ubba yellida. Phawuloosara yedhdhize Maqedooniya asuntsana, Gaayoosan Arsxirokoosan aykkii gochchiter kaa7ize bessa woxxida.
ACT 19:30 Phawuloosan asuntsi shiiqide besite gelodes koyda, yezin ammanzuntsi eza kayda.
ACT 19:31 Isiya sa7a hyalaquntsappa Phawuloosa lagge maaqqide fete fete Phawuloosago kiittii, «Kaasi besite qoncce kezii benttippe» ga7i eza woossida.
ACT 19:32 Shiiqide asuntsi hyanodebaz dhabida; gaanggize bagga asuntsi melle atto yezin akkos shiiqezako eroosse gisho fete fettibazis uukkize wode hyankkay mellebazis uukkane.
ACT 19:33 Ayhuduntsi Iskkinddire gaaze atstsa aatsii beezin, fettii fettii asuntsi E gawude baz ohi eza tiino aatsida. E asuntsi si77i gawude gaar fa kushite mallii beezi, asuntsis mootinttodes eqqida.
ACT 19:34 Yezin Iskkinddire Ayhude asi maaqqidanno asuntsi eride wode lam77i saate maaqqade gaar ubbuntsi fettii qaalara, «Efesoone Arxemiise damma» ga7i uukkida.
ACT 19:35 Wurssutsite Katama xaafize asuntsana si77i yiizii, «Efesoone asuntso! Efesoone katama damma Arxemiise eeqa keetstsin saloppa wodhdhide damma shuchchiza naagizanno eroosse asi baaya.
ACT 19:36 Hyanno kaddize asi baayze gisho yin si77i ga7odesin ellisii akko baz yiizaanxxi ashshodes beezane.
ACT 19:37 Yin hyantsi asuntsana, eeqa keetstsa bira kaystikaayzuntsanan nu Xoozza cazikaayzuntsana ki7i.
ACT 19:38 Yinnii gisho, Dimexiroosan eera yeze oochchize asuntsi mootodes oona koyzako, firdda keetsita bugutsi yene; daynnuntsin yene; un mootodes dandda7ane.
ACT 19:39 Yezin yin melle ohe koyko, Shanggo shiiqite ohita bi7intto.
ACT 19:40 Yinno maaqqanxiko hyayno hyanide bazis Roome ka7itumtta nuna oocoda. Hyanna buqutsitis miknaate baayze gisho nu mikinaato ohodes dandda7oos»
ACT 19:41 yaga7i shiiqito lalida.
ACT 20:1 Uukita si7i gaydannippa suuba Phawuloosa ammanze asuntsana xeegizi unttana zorii mintsitsidannippa suuba saritstsi Maqedoona qitodes kezida.
ACT 20:2 E aadhize sa7a yeze ammanze asuntsis qaala ohi mintsitsidannippa suuba Girike sa7a qitida.
ACT 20:3 E ize hyaydzdzii agina bettii, markkabera Sooriya qitodes qoppii yezin, Ayhuduntsi fana wodhodes koyizanno erii Maqedooniyara suub maaqqades koyda.
ACT 20:4 Phawuloosa moyziduntsi Beeriyappa Pharhuusa na7aya Sophaxiroosa, Teselonqeppa Arsxirokoosan Sikondduusa, Derbbeppa Gaayoosa, Iisiyappa Tikiqoosa, Xirofimoosan Ximotiyoosan.
ACT 20:5 Hyantses tiino hyanggi nuna Xiro7aadalla kafane.
ACT 20:6 Nu Boora Ba7ale bonchchidannippa suuba Filphisiyusappa markkabera denddii, ichchintsa qammara unttana Xiro7aada yellii ize laappun qamma gam77ida.
ACT 20:7 Saaminttappa tiino qamma nu boora baxxodes shiiqii yezin, Phawuloosa wonttistto qitodes qoppide gisho unttis qaala ohitera giddii bilahe yellodes ohito gam7izida.
ACT 20:8 Nu shiiqii bettide fooqite gaama foo7o yene.
ACT 20:9 Ewuxikoosa gaaze fettii yidhdhize maskkootella bettii, fana botii genttida. Phawuloosa ohito pharggizide wode Ewuxikoosa gentti hyaydzdzintsa fooqizeppa gol7i hyayqqezin asuntsi dentsida.
ACT 20:10 Yezin Phawuloosa wodhdhii, eella zuggida. Eza iringgi, «E hyayqqikaaya, tannippete» gayda.
ACT 20:11 Yinnippa suuba, ude fooqella kezii boora baxxi mu7ida. Sa7a wonttode wontsis asuntsis ohidannippa suuba denddii qitida.
ACT 20:12 Ye faxide yidhdhiza kara kanggi gaama ufayttida.
ACT 20:13 Yezin Phawuloosa fana izippa mokkode gaar nuus ohide gisho tiinidhii markkabego hyanggi, Asoosa qitodes denddida. Akkos gayko, E tohera qitodes qoppide gisho nuna hyannii gaar kiittida.
ACT 20:14 E nuura Asoosa yellinttin markkabera eza ekkii Mixiliine hyanggida.
ACT 20:15 Wonttistti wode izippa denddii markkabera Kiyoosa tiino yeze besite yellida; mahi wonttistti wode Saamosa fiinggi kaallize wodite Miliixe yellida.
ACT 20:16 Phawuloosa Isiya gidda gaama gami7ikaayzara Efesoone kalera aadhodes qoppida. Faas dandda7inttiko Phenxeqosxe Ba7ale wode Yerusalaame yellodes ellisane.
ACT 20:17 Phawuloosa Miliixeppa Efesoone kiittii woosa keetstsa cimuntsana xeegizida.
ACT 20:18 Woosa keetstsa cimuntsi eego yi7in, unttago hyannigaara yagayda: «Taanii Isiya gelide tiino qammitippa aykkii yinttara yezide wode ubba wayzi yezezako yin erane.
ACT 20:19 Ayhuduntsi shiiqii taalla madha yeltsikon ta ashkketitsaran gaama afutstsara Laatstsis oochchida.
ACT 20:20 Bucan yin keetsite keetsite yinttana tamaarssittera yinttana maaddize bazappa fettibazin faccizikaaya.
ACT 20:21 Taanii Ayhuduntsisin Ayhude maaqqoosuntsis nagarappa Xoozago maaqqade gaaran nu Laatstse Yesuusa ammanode gaar markkidhida.
ACT 20:22 «Ize tana akko yellode yezako eroos, yezin hyatte taanii Geeshi Ayyaanas kiitinttii Yerusalaame qitane.
ACT 20:23 Yinno maaqqikon Geeshi Ayyaana katama ubba achchin madhan tana naagizanno taas markkidhida.
ACT 20:24 Yezin ta wotsito folodes Laatstse Yesuusap ekkide oochito, Xoozze aadho keehatitsi Wonggele markkidhizanno folodes ta shemppito fatstsoosse baz fana faydane.
ACT 20:25 «Taanii hyatten Xoozze ka7itumo markkidhitera yin gidda wutida. Yikkeppa suuba yinttappa ooden tana be7aamanno erane.
ACT 20:26 Yinnii gisho, yinttappa fettii asi dhabikon ta oocinttaamanno hyayno qamma yinttis geeshi ohine.
ACT 20:27 Akkos gayko, Xoozze qofa ubba yinttis akko bazin ashshikaayzara ohida.
ACT 20:28 «Fa na7ay suutsite wonggide Xoozze woosa keetsito naagote. Geeshi Ayyaana yinttana yenggizuntsana mahi dooride wuditisin yin ommitisin naaginttote.
ACT 20:29 Taanii hyanggidannippa suuba, wuditis yiqsinttoosse iita suudhumuntsi yin gidda gelodanno ta erane.
ACT 20:30 Tamaaruntsana fa suub kaalitsodes worddo tamaarssize asuntsi yin giddappa denddoda.
ACT 20:31 Yinnii gisho, ta hyaydzdzii bere qamman awaran afutstsara yinttana ommite ommite kaccidanno qoppitter minggote.
ACT 20:32 «Hyatten yinttana mintsodesin geeshi asuntsara laata immades dandda7ize Xoozzesin E aadho keehatitsi qaalas yinttana hyadara inggane.
ACT 20:33 «Taanii oodeppan bira woy worqqa woy afula ekkikaaya.
ACT 20:34 Taanii ta kushite oochchii taasin taara yezuntsana beezzebaz maaddidanno yin, yin ommite erane.
ACT 20:35 Yin hyannifana labbii oochitera labbiduntsana maaddodannon Laatstsii Yesuusa, ‹Ekkizeppa aadhii inggizay anjjinttidaya› gayde qaaltto yin qoppodes beezanno ta yinttana ubbabazite beezida» yagayda.
ACT 20:36 Phawuloosa yinno ohi hyaasii un ubbuntsara bunqqunttii Xooz woossida.
ACT 20:37 Un ubbuntsi Phawuloosa iringgi yeekkii yeerida.
ACT 20:38 E Mahi, «Tana be7aama» yagayde qaaltta unttana gaama azzantsida. Un markkabe yellodes eza moyzida.
ACT 21:1 Nu Efesoone cimuntsappa shaginttideppa suuba markkabera Qoose qitida. Wonttistti wode Rooda yellii izippa Phaxira qitida.
ACT 21:2 Fenqqe fiinggize markkabe denggi E gidda gelii qitodes denddida.
ACT 21:3 Nu Qoophiroosa bi7ide wode, Qoophiroosa workkita bagga ashshii Sooriya yedhdhida. Markkabize fa caantto ize ketstsodes koyde gisho Xiroosa qitida.
ACT 21:4 Ize ammanze asuntsana denggi unttara laappun qamma bettida. Phawuloosa Yerusalaame qitaame gaar un ees Ayyaanara ohida.
ACT 21:5 Nuunii un kale gam7ize wodita hyal7in kezii qitida. Un ubba fa machchuntsaran fa na7untsara wolla katamappa gaxa kessii nuna moyzida. Nu abba kale bunqqunttii Xooz woossida.
ACT 21:6 Yinnippa suuba, wol sarotsin nu markkabite gelida; un fa kara maaqqida.
ACT 21:7 Nu abba ogito hyaasii, Xiroosappa Phexelemaysa yellida. Ize ammanze asuntsana saritstsi, un kale fettii qamma feezhida.
ACT 21:8 Wonttistti wode kezii, Qisaariya qitida. Sabaake Filphoosa kara yellii E kale bettida. E Yerusalaame tiino doorinttide laappuntsafa feta.
ACT 21:9 Filphoosas nabe maaqqide oyddii wudur na7untsi yene.
ACT 21:10 Nuunii unddenna qamma ize bettezin Agaboosa gaaze nabe Yihudappa Qisaariya yi7ida.
ACT 21:11 Nuugo yi7i Phawuloosa saqqe ekkii nabize fa kushiton fa tohito accii, «Geeshi Ayyaana hyay saqqize adaya, Yerusalaame Ayhuduntsi hyannigaara accii, Ayhude maaqqoosse asuntsis aatsii inggoda gaane» yagayda.
ACT 21:12 Nuunii yinno si7ide wode nuunin yeze asuntsi Phawuloosa Yerusalaame qitaame gaar woossida.
ACT 21:13 Yezin Phawuloosa mahi, «Yin hyannigaara yeekkitera akkos ta wozintto tannize? Taanii, Laatstse Yesuusa suntsiti gisho acintte xalaala maaqqikaayzin Yerusalaame hyayqqodesin giiginttida» yagayda.
ACT 21:14 Nu zoridanno E ekkanxi ixxin, «Laatstse qofita hyano» ga7i si77i gayda.
ACT 21:15 Ize eeratsi wode gam77idannippa suuba giiginttii Yerusalaame qitodes kezida.
ACT 21:16 Qisaariya yeze ammanze asuntsappa eeratsuntsi nuura hyanggida. Un nuunii shemppode bessi Minaasone gaaze Qoophiroosa atstse kara kaalitsida. Minaasone tiino ammanide asuntsappa feta.
ACT 21:17 Nuunii Yerusalaame yellide wode ammanze asuntsi nuna ufaytti mokkida.
ACT 21:18 Wonttistti wode Phawuloosan nuunii Yayqoobara yellinttodes qitida. Woosa keetstsa cimuntsi ubbuntsi ize yene.
ACT 21:19 Phawuloosa unttana saritstsidannippa suuba Ayhude maaqqoosse asunts gidda fa baggara Xoozii oochchidanno ubba unttis ohida.
ACT 21:20 Un yinno si7ide wode Xooz galatii Phawuloosago hyannigaara yagayda: «Nu ishayo, Ayhuduntsi gidda wantsi mukuluntsi Xooz ammanezako ne be7ine; un ubbuntsin higge mintsii naagane.
ACT 21:21 Neenii Ayhude maaqqoosuntsana sa7a yeze Ayhude ubba fa na7untsi garrazinttaame gaar, Ayhuduntsi woga kaallaame gaaran Muse higge ixxode gaar neenii tamaarssizanno Yerusalaame yeze Ayhuduntsi si7ida.
ACT 21:22 Yeezin akko lo77o? Ne yi7idanno turo si7oda.
ACT 21:23 «Yinnii gisho, nuunii nees ohizanno si7o; gefa yeze oyddii asuntsi nu kale yene.
ACT 21:24 Unttana ekkii unttara geezho; mahi un fa ommito meedinttode gaar unttis miishe inggo. Un zaga nebaz si7idanna turo maaqqikaayzannon neenii ne ommiten higge naagize asi maaqqidanno ubbuntsi erane.
ACT 21:25 «Yezin ammanze Ayhude maaqqoosse asuntsana maaqqizako, un eeqas zharshinttidebaz ma7aame gaar, suutsi uzhaame gaar, bawuta ma7aame gaaran olalaame gaar, nuunii ohito accii, firddi unttis kiita xaafida» gayda.
ACT 21:26 Yinnippa suuba, Phawuloosa wonttistti wode asuntsana ekkii, unttara geezhida. E fa geezhe wodita ayde folinttode yezako erisodesin fa zharshito ayde zharshode yezako erisodes Xoozze keetstsa gelida.
ACT 21:27 Laappun qamma folinttodes ukkodera, Iisiyappa yi7ide Ayhuduntsi Xoozze Keetstsa Phawuloosa bi7i, as ubba dentsitsii Phawuloosa aykkida.
ACT 21:28 «Isra7eele asuntso, nuna maaddote; hyay atstse, nu worzhito, nu higgiton hyanna Xoozze Keetsito ixxode gaar as ubbuntsana ubba bessa tamaarssane. Yinnan maaqqaanxi ixxin Ayhude maaqqoosuntsana Xoozze keetstsa gelitsii, hyanna geeshi bessito tunizida» yaga7i uukkida.
ACT 21:29 Un yinno gaydanna zaga Efesoone Xirofimoosa Phawuloosara katama bi7ide gisho hyatte Phawuloosa Xoozze keetstsa eza ekkii gelidebaz unttis aazida.
ACT 21:30 Katamita ubba buqinttida; asuntsi ubba shiiqii Phawuloosa aykkii Xoozze keetstsappa bale gochchida. Xoozze Keetstsa furtsita ellisii gorddinttida.
ACT 21:31 Asuntsi Phawuloosa wodhodes yi7adera, «Yerusalaame katama kumutsi buqinttida» gaaze wortta Roome shaalaqago yellida.
ACT 21:32 Shaalaqize wottaddaruntsanan mato hyalaquntsana ekkii woxxittera yi7ida. Asuntsi shaalaqizan wottaddaruntsana bi7ide wode Phawuloosa guuddizanno ashshida.
ACT 21:33 Ye wode shaalaqize shiiqii, Phawuloosa aykkii, lam77i santsalaatara acinttode gaar kiittida. Yeyzi, E oona yezakon akko oochchezako asuntsana oocida.
ACT 21:34 Asuntsappa baggita fettibaz ga7i uukkize wode hyankuntsi mellebaz ga7i uukkane. Uukita gaanggide gisho shaalaqize turtto shagodes dandda7inttaanxin, wottaddaruntsi Phawuloosa fa yeze bessa kanggode gaar kiittida.
ACT 21:35 Phawuloosa yedhdhii kezize darajjito yellize wode asuntsi urqqizanni gisho wottaddaruntsi eza tookkida.
ACT 21:36 Gaama asuntsi, «E hyayqqo!» ga7i uukkitera kaallane.
ACT 21:37 Wottaddaruntsi Phawuloosa fa yeze bessito geltsodes yi7adera, Phawuloosa shaalaqizego, «Taanii nees fettibaz ohiko si7odate?» gayda. E Phawuloosago, «Ne Girike doona erane?
ACT 21:38 Neenii hyannippa tiino buqutsi medhdhii shemppo wodhide oyddii mukul asuntsana ekkii akko baayze ganas gelide Gibxxe atstsa baane?» gayda.
ACT 21:39 Yezin Phawuloosa, «Taanii, Kilqiya yeze erinttide Terseese katama asi maaqqide Ayhude asi. Tana asuntsis ohizoya?» gayda.
ACT 21:40 Shaalaqize eego, «Oho» ga7in Phawuloosa darajjalla eqqii, asuntsi si77i gawude gaar fa kushtira mallida. Asuntsi si77i ga7in Ibraysxe doonara hyannigaara gayda:
ACT 22:1 «Ta ishuntson, ta aduntso, taanii hyatte yinttis inggize mahito si7ote.»
ACT 22:2 Phawuloosa unttis Ibraysxe doonara ohizanna si7i kasennippa aatsii si77i gayda. E kaallii,
ACT 22:3 «Taanii Kilqiya yeze Terseese yelintti hyanna katamtte diccida. Ta asttamaarizen Gamaaliyale; taanii nu aaduntsi higgito mintsii tamaarida, hyayno yin ubba hyanizannigaara Xoozis mishinttize Ayhude asi.
ACT 22:4 Ta hyanna ogito kaallize maachuntsanan dhiiratsunsana aykkii achi keetstsa oliteran unttana wodhissade wontsis madha beezze asi.
ACT 22:5 Yinnii gaara, kahinunts hyalaqizen Shanggo ubba ta baz markkidhades dandda7ane. Taanii Damasqqo yeze un ishuntsis unttappa dabddaabbe ekkii ize yeze asuntsi acinttii seerinttode gaar Yerusalaame unttana ko7odes ize qitida.
ACT 22:6 «Ta hyanggi Damasqqo ukkide wode awara saate qoppikaayzin saloppa damma foo7o ta kantto wutii foo7ida.
ACT 22:7 Ta sa7ite gol7i yessadera, ‹Saawula, Saawula, tana akkos baytstse?› gaaze qaala si7ida.
ACT 22:8 Taanii mahi, ‹Laatstso, neenii oode?› yagayda. «E mahi, Taanii, ne baytsize Naazirete Yesuusa» yagayda.
ACT 22:9 Taara yezuntsi foo7ito bi7idap attin taas ohize qaaltto si7ikaaya.
ACT 22:10 «Taanii, ‹Laatstso, ta akko oochcho?› yagayda. «Laatstsi taago, ‹Denddii Damasqqo qito. Ne oochchode gaar Xoozii qoppidebaz ubba ize nees ohinttoda› yagayda.
ACT 22:11 Yinna damma foo7itippa denddii ta aafita dhumin, taara yeze asuntsi ta kushito aykkii, tana gochchii Damasqqo yeltstsida.
ACT 22:12 «Damasqqo yeze Ayhuduntsi ubba markkidhezen gaama bonchchize fettii Hananiya gaaze atstse, nu higgito bonchchizen Xooz mintsii woossize yene.
ACT 22:13 E taago yi7i, ta kale eqqii, ‹Ta ishe Saawula, bo7o› gayda. Ellisii ta eza bi7ida.
ACT 22:14 «E taago, ‹Nu aaduntsi Xoozze neenii E qoftto erode gaar, Xilliza be7ade gaaran E doonttippa qaala si7ade gaar tiinii nena doorida.
ACT 22:15 Neenii bi7idebazisin si7idebaz as ubba tiino ees markka maaqqade fana.
ACT 22:16 Hyatte akkos gam77e? Xammaqintto; E suntsito xeegii ne nagarttippa meecintto› yagayda.
ACT 22:17 «Taanii suuba Yerusalaame maaqqii Xoozze Keetstsa woossodera, taas qonccitsi benttida.
ACT 22:18 Qonccisite Laatstsii taago, ‹Ne taas markkidhize markkatitsito asuntsi ekkoosse gisho ellisii Yerusalaameppa kezo› yaga7odera bi7ida.
ACT 22:19 «Taanii, ‹Laatstso, Ayhude woosa Keetstsa ubba nena ammanzuntsana aykkii hyadhdhidayan achi keetstsa olidaya maaqqizanno un erane.
ACT 22:20 Un ne markka Isxifaanosa wodhize wode ta yinna oochchite wolla yene. Mahi un kale eqqii eza wodhizunts ma7ito naagane› yagayda.
ACT 22:21 «Laatstsii taago, ‹Taanii nena Ayhude maaqqoosse asuntsago hyaako sa7a kiittode gisho denddii qito› » yagayda.
ACT 22:22 Phawuloosa yinna qaaltto ohi hyaasode wontsis asuntsi E gaazanno si7ine. Yinnippa suuba, fa qaaltto dhoqi yiizii, «Hyanna sa7itippa dhabiso! E yessades beezoos» yagayda.
ACT 22:23 Un kacinttii, fa ma7ito eella afa dhogii xura ude lalodera;
ACT 22:24 Shaalaqize bi7i wottaddaruntsi Phawuloosa un fa yeze bessa kanggode gaara kiitida. Mahi asuntsi akkos hyannigaara kacinttezako erodes koyi Phawuloosa dafera garafii loytsii oocode gaar unttana kiittida.
ACT 22:25 Yezin wottaddaruntsi Phawuloosa dafera mintsii accii garafodes yiize wode Phawuloosa fa kantte eqqide mato hyalaqizego, «Roome asi firdda baayzin garafizanna yinttis woga?» yagayda.
ACT 22:26 Mato hyalaqize yinno si7ide wode shaalaqizego hyanggi, «Hyay atstse Roome asi. Neenii akko oochchodes qoppe?» yaga7i oocida.
ACT 22:27 Shaalaqize Phawuloosago shiiqii, «Ne Roome aso? Ane taas oho» yagayda. Phawuloosa, «Yee» yagayda.
ACT 22:28 Shaalaqize mahi, «Taanii hyanno gadetitsito gaama miishera ekkida» yagayda. Yezin Phawuloosa, «Ta hyanna gadetitsito yelintti ekkida» yagayda.
ACT 22:29 Yinnii gisho, Phawuloosa loytsii oocodes qoppiduntsi iira eeppa shaakkinttida. Shaalaqize Roome asi santsalaatara accidanno eride wode zhashtida.
ACT 22:30 Wonttisti wode Shaalaqize, Ayhuduntsi Phawuloosa akkos mootezako shaakkii erodes koyi billida. Kahinunts hyalaquntsin shanggo ubbuntsi shiiqode gaar kiittida; mahi Phawuloosa ki7i un tiino essida.
ACT 23:1 Phawuloosa firddize asuntsana dakkii bi7i, «Ta ishuntso, ta hyayno yellodes Xoozze tiino ta yestte ubba lo77o wozinara yezida» gayda.
ACT 23:2 Kahinunts hyalaqize Hananiya, Phawuloosa doontto baqqode gaar E kale eqqiduntsana kiittida.
ACT 23:3 Ye wode Phawuloosa eego, «Naate bootsi forchcho tizhinttide dochey, Xoozii nena baqqoda. Neenii taalla higgera firddodes bettii yezite higge ashshii tana baqqade gaar kiittane?» yagayda.
ACT 23:4 Phawuloosa kale eqqiduntsi eego, «Ne Xoozze kahinunts hyalaqa cazhane?» yagayda.
ACT 23:5 Phawuloosa, «Ta ishuntso, E kahinunts hyalaqa maaqqidanno ta erikaaya; akkos gayko Xoozze qaaltte, ‹Ne worzha ahizella iita qaala ohippe› yaga7intti xaafinttida» yagayda.
ACT 23:6 Yezin Phawuloosa yinna besite yeze asuntsappa bagguntsi Saduqaawuyane, bagguntsi Farisaawuyane maaqqizanno erii, «Ta ishuntso, ta Farisaawuyane Farisaawuyane na7a; ‹Hyayqqiduntsi hyayqoppa denddoda› ga7i taanii ufayssara naagize gisho un taalla firddane» yaga7i ohida.
ACT 23:7 Phawuloosa yinno gayde wode Farisaawunts giddan Saduqaawuntsi gidda kachchi kezin shaakkinttida.
ACT 23:8 Akkos gayko, Saduqaawuntsi, «Hyayqqide asi denddoos; kiitanchchon, ayyaanan baaya» yagaazuntsana. Yezin Farisaawuntsi ubba yezanno ammanane.
ACT 23:9 Damma kachchi kezida; Farisaawunts zala maaqqide higge asttamaaruntsi denddii eqqii, «Hyay atstsella akko bala baz denggikaaya; ees ayyaana woy kiitanchcho ohikaayzara ashshoos» yaga7i wolla lallida.
ACT 23:10 Kachchita ganggin asuntsi Phawuloosa shaqitsi ekkaame gaar ga7i, shaalaqize fa wottaddaruntsi wodhdhii un gidda fa eza ellisii kessii fa yeze bessa kanggode gaar kiittida.
ACT 23:11 Yinnii qamma Laatstsii Phawuloosa kale eqqii, «Phawuloosa, ne taas Yerusalaame markkidhidanni fana Roomen markkidhades beezane; minggo; akko baaya» yagayda.
ACT 23:12 Wonttisti wode Ayhuduntsi, «Phawuloosa wodhikaayzara mo7oos uzhoos» ga7i caaqqida.
ACT 23:13 Phawuloosalla yinno zorintti caaqqide asuntsi oytamappa aadhane.
ACT 23:14 Un kahinunts hyalaquntsi gade cimuntsago hyanggi, «Nuunii Phawuloosa wodhikaayzara katstsa gaazebaz mo7oos ga7i caaqqida.
ACT 23:15 Yikke, yinttin shangguntsin E baz loytsii qurichchizebaz yeze baz mahi, Phawuloosa yinttago ko7ode gaar shaalaqiza oocote. Nuunii E hyanna shiiqita yellodannippa tiino eza wodhodes giigii bettida» yagayda.
ACT 23:16 Yezin Phawuloosa mishti na7ay yinna zorinttidanno si7i hyanggi wottaddaruntsi yeze bessito gelii, Phawuloosas ohida.
ACT 23:17 Phawuloosa mato hyalaquntsappa feta xeegii, «Hyay na7aya shaalaqizes ohize baz yeze gisho eza shaalaqizego kanggo» gayda.
ACT 23:18 Mato hyalaqize na7aya shaalaqizego kanggi, «Achi keetstsa yeze Phawuloosa tana faago xeegii, hyay na7ay nees ohize baz yeze gisho eza neego ko7ode gaar tana woossida» yagayda.
ACT 23:19 Shaalaqize na7ay kushito aykkii, bale kessii, «Ne taas ohode qoftta akko?» yaga7i oocida.
ACT 23:20 Na7ay shaalaqizego, «Ayhuduntsi Phawuloosabaz tiinoppan miintsii qurichchodes koyze gaar aazin neenii wontta eza shiiqite ko7ode gaar nena woossodes zore accida.
ACT 23:21 Yezin neenii un gaazanno si7ippe. Akkos gayko, oytamappa aadhize asuntsi Phawuloosa wodhikaayzara ‹Katstsa mo7oos, hyaatsi uzhoos› ga7i caaqqii, aachintti eza kafane. Hyatte ne gaazebaz xalaala si7odes kafane» yagayda.
ACT 23:22 Shaalaqize mahi, «Hyanna ohito ne taas ohidanno melle oodesin ohippe» yaga7i na7aya suub dakkida.
ACT 23:23 Shaalaqize mato hyalaquntsappa lam77untsana xeegii, «Qammappa hyaydzdzii saate Qisaariya qitodes, lam77i xeet wottaddaruntsana, laappun tam faara asuntsanan lam77i xeet toora woringgizuntsana giigizote.
ACT 23:24 Gadito ahize Filkkisago Phawuloosa saro yelitsodes toggize faara giigizote» yaga7i unttana kiittida.
ACT 23:25 Shaalaqize Filkkisas hyannigaara gaaze dabddaabbe xaafida:
ACT 23:26 «Qalawudiyoosa Luusiyosappa gade ahize bonchcho Filkkisasa, saro nees maaqqe.
ACT 23:27 Ayhuduntsi hyay atstsa aykkii wodhodes yi7adera, E Roome sa7a asi maaqqidanno erii wottaddaruntsara yellii eza ashshida.
ACT 23:28 Un eza akkos mootizako erodes koyi un shiiqite eza ta shiishida.
ACT 23:29 Un fa higgitis eza mootidap attin eza wodhizebaz woy accizebaz baayzanno ta denggida.
